This November

A Comet Will Appear in the Far East

丨Accompanied by Peculiar Phenomena丨

Thousands of Meteors Will Fall With It

World News Agency, New York - A comet named "Tempel" has not been seen on Earth for 33 years. According to calculations by astronomers, this comet will reappear in November this year, and it will be most clearly visible in China and Japan. Regarding this appearance, it will be accompanied by a peculiar phenomenon, that is, at the same time, a large group of meteors will fly and fall on the Earth. The comet's closest approach to the ground is estimated to be on November 17 and 18. According to reports, the "Tempel" comet approached the Earth in August 1898, and at that time, it could only be observed scientifically on the east coast of North America and a part of the Atlantic Ocean. This year, it can be clearly seen in Japan and China between 2:00 and 3:00 in the afternoon of November 17 and 18, and it can be seen without the help of a telescope. As for the visible meteors, there will be as many as 1,000 in 6 hours.

German Doctors Invent Brain Tonic

National News Agency, Berlin, 15th - Two famous German medical scientists, Professor Kronfeld and Professor Voigt, announced today that they have tested a so-called brain tonic with very good results. They used it on six ordinary people, and after strict testing, their intelligence increased by 50%. However, the average increase was only 20%. It only took 6 hours and 25 minutes to complete 8 hours of work.

News Briefs

Bandit Suppression Army 3

Continuously Capture Yingshan and Shangcheng

Hankou Correspondence - The 47th Division of Shangguan Yunxiang and the 54th Division of Hao Mengling were ordered to advance towards Yingshan from Qiguang and other places in eastern Hubei. The area originally belonged to Anhui Province, but it was temporarily assigned to Hubei for the convenience of suppression. Shangguan's division captured Jiming River on the 12th and fought hard to recapture Fangjiazu, the second gateway to Yingshan, that night. Hao's division also set out from Yejia River in the rain and occupied important passes such as Ping'anling, Fenghuanggua, and Mengmengshan on the 13th, and joined Shangguan to advance. They then arrived near Yingshan County and seized the hills. The Red bandits resisted stubbornly. From morning to noon, the bandit forces did not stop and all retreated into the city. The artillery of the unit concentrated its firepower and first destroyed the important passes on the city. The vanguard troops then broke through the south gate under the cover of artillery fire and machine guns. The bandits could not defend and fled north in embarrassment from the Xihua River. The bandits at Jimingjian also withdrew from the Donghua River at the same time. The National Army completely captured Yingshan County at 3:00 pm that day. They searched for the remnants of the bandits, comforted the people, and dispatched left and right wings to follow up from Jinjiapu Yangliubian. Shangguan Yunxiang, the commander of the 47th Division, received the report at the Qishui military camp late at night and telegraphed Hankou to report the victory. The text said, "Our army completely occupied Yingshan at 2:00 pm today. The remnants of the false 5th Division and the independent 13th Regiment of the false guerrillas retreated in different directions towards Jinjiazai and Huoshan. Our army is pursuing and cleaning up at the same time. In this battle, hundreds of bandits were killed and many were captured. They are being cleared up. The bullet factory manufactured by the Yingshan Red bandits was also intercepted and destroyed." As for the central route, after the recapture of Xinji, most of the Red bandits entrenched in Shangcheng as their last bastion. Jinjiaji, not far from Shangcheng, was their most important defense line, stationed with the false 10th Division, the Shangcheng Independent Division, the Guangshan Independent Division, and other Red Guards, claiming tens of thousands of people. At 4:00 pm on the 13th, they fought fiercely with the central route of the National Army, the 2nd Column, at Qiligang Suishicun. The National Army detoured to its right wing and attacked the flanks from the side. The bandits suffered heavy losses and were all defeated. They retreated to the Yujiaji fortress. The National Army took advantage of the victory and advanced sharply, engaged in hand-to-hand combat and climbed the fortress one after another. They finally broke through and occupied Yujiaji at 7:00 pm. Another part also captured Gedian Sanliudian and went straight to Shangcheng. The place had deep trenches and high fortresses, making it even more difficult to attack. On the evening of the 13th, the 1st and 2nd Columns of the central route of the National Army marched lightly and urgently and launched a night attack on Shangcheng. The Red bandits were caught off guard and the 1st Column broke into the southwest city gate. The bandits, seeing that the strong city had been broken, scrambled to escape, trampling on each other, causing countless deaths and injuries. Many were killed by the National Army. A part of them broke out of the city and were also intercepted. Thousands of people were captured. The above is the area of the central route army in eastern Hubei and southern Henan. Now, it is only necessary to connect with the right-wing army and capture the bandit nest of Jinjiazai, and the bandit suppression military affairs on this route can be concluded. (September 14)

Harbin Flood Gradually Recedes 4

Japanese Still Ignore the Disaster Situation Outside Daoli

Bao Guancheng and Zhang Jinghui Compete for Power

Japanese Military Police Humiliates the Chief Inspector to Death

Harbin Correspondence - Since the great flood in this area, the weather has been rainy recently, but it clears up soon. The upstream mountain torrents have been washed away, and the river water has fallen slightly. Since the flood, the water level has dropped by about 57 centimeters. The Flood Disaster Extraordinary Committee organized by the puppet government in Daoli has ordered the manufacture of ten drainage machines. Since the installation and implementation of drainage, the accumulated water in the city streets has been decreasing day by day. The southern end of Central Avenue and Xincheng Avenue is still not completely drained due to low-lying areas, but the water level has been reduced to about a foot. The water depth in the artillery team and Zhengyang River partial warehouses is still three or four feet or more. It will take about half a month to completely drain. Although the accumulated water outside Daoli has dropped since the river water receded, it has only decreased by one foot and five or six inches so far. East of Wuliu and Liuliu Streets, the water depth is still submerged. Merchants and gentry outside Daoli have repeatedly urged the puppet water committee to drain the water and relieve the market. Until recently, there was a proposal to start on September 20 and drain the water by October 20. However, the number of drainage machines needs to be increased to 21 to be effective within 30 days. In addition to the Chamber of Commerce trying to raise funds, the puppet water committee is rushing to manufacture them. Before the implementation of the drainage work, sandbags and wooden stakes were used to block a section of the embankment that collapsed on the Jiangdi 90th Street. This matter started on September 1. Four rows of sandbags were piled up to form an arc, and wooden stakes were nailed outside to prevent the water from washing them away. It is estimated that it will take four days to complete. The river water is currently about half a foot below the brick dam. The puppet water committee plans to wait until the water drops to 20 centimeters below the dam before draining the water. According to the Chamber of Commerce and various public groups, it is proposed to ask various ships to help by using the pumps on each ship to help drain the water. It can be drained mostly in about a week. The puppet water committee does not allow it, saying that the drainage plan is determined by the committee and other parties may not change it. The Chamber of Commerce and other groups painfully watched the losses and did not dare to argue. Later, it was learned that the acting chairman of the puppet water committee, Hirata (Hirata, the chief advisor to the puppet chief official's office and the municipal preparation office), colluded with Russian engineers and secretly accepted bribes, ordering the Russians to handle the matter. At the same time, the Japanese were gloating over the disaster of the Chinese. Therefore, although tens of millions of merchants outside Daoli were in the midst of the flood, Hirata never cared about it. Bao Guancheng, the puppet mayor, also served as the chairman of the puppet construction propaganda committee. Recently, he has been corrupting the organization of Greater Harbin and competing with Zhang Jinghui, the chief executive of the puppet special zone, for power. The undercurrent is very strong. Because the flood flooded Harbin, Zhang Jinghui complained to the Japanese that Bao was fond of doing good deeds and vying for credit, and the authority was not unified by him, which caused an unprecedented disaster. The Japanese believed it and transferred Bao to serve as a representative stationed in Japan, which was a clear promotion but a secret demotion. His vacancy was filled by Lu Ronghuan, who could take over around the 15th. Bao wanted to resign and not go because he was appointed to be a representative in Japan, which was a job that suffered the most. The Japanese did not allow it, so he complained a lot behind his back, saying that working with the Japanese was like living with tigers and wolves and could not predict when their beastly nature would erupt. Lu Ronghuan was the superintendent of the Eastern Railway who caused the Middle-Eastern Railway Incident in 1929. This gangster retired and lived at home and did not deeply conceal himself. After the establishment of the puppet country, he tried his best to run around. At first, he sought the superintendent of the Middle-Eastern Railway, but he opposed it. Later, he tried hard to get the mayor of Harbin, and now he has got his wish.

In this great flood, one person sacrificed, and the narration is quite pitiful. It can also be a warning to the great husbands of the subjugated country. The chief inspector of the Binjiang puppet public security bureau, Liu Zhao, ordered the police to patrol in shifts every day after the flood entered the city. He did not dare to slack off day and night. His achievements in the local area cannot be denied because he was an official of the subjugated country. Unexpectedly, at the end of July, because a certain inspector under his command was absent from duty, a Japanese military police sergeant, Maeda, slapped his face in public, and went to the flooded market barefooted to wade in the water to explore the depth. Liu was slightly distant, and Maeda beat him up in the street. At that time, there were many onlookers. Liu was seriously injured by the beating. After returning home, he became ill due to anger, and lingered for more than 20 days before dying. After his death, the Japanese military police forbade the coffin from being placed in the house and forced it to be buried quickly. His family had no choice but to bury him hastily. Liu had been the section chief and chief inspector of the public security bureau for nearly eight years and had never made a mistake. Unexpectedly, because he was demoted to an official of the puppet country, he was humiliated to death by a small soldier. It is also sad. (September 7)

Anhui Tea Merchants Oppose 5

Jiangxi Levies Throughput Production and Sales Tax on Anhui Tea

Wuyuan Correspondence - Yangzhuang red and green box tea of Huizhou is the largest export of Anhui Province. In recent years, in order to take care of the difficulties of tea merchants and promote the development of foreign trade of Chinese tea, the government has completely exempted the Lishui tax on exported box tea. The reason why Chinese tea does not disappear from the European and American markets is half dependent on this relief. This year, the Anhui Provincial Government has set up a special tea tax in various tea-producing counties. The tax rate on box tea has been changed to 20% of the value. After the opposition of all tea merchants, it was changed back to the 19th-year case, collecting 1 yuan, 1 jiao, 2 fen and 5 li per 100 catties of lead. Tea merchants believe that the restoration of the previous lead system will stop the opposition. Last month, thousands of boxes of box tea from Wuyuan's various terminal gangs were transported through Xiangtan, Dexing. The Jingwei team there suddenly blocked the box tea, drawing 8 jiao per box, because the Qingxiang funds were insufficient. Tea merchants refused to pay this illegal and harsh tax, which almost caused a great disturbance. Recently, the Hukou Investigation Office of the Jiujiang Collection Bureau of Special Products Production and Sales in Jiangxi Province has also forcibly collected production and sales taxes on box tea passing through Wuyuan, collecting 1 yuan, 1 jiao, 2 fen and 5 li per 100 catties according to the lead system. The tea house tea guests all said that this box tea is produced in Anhui Province. The Anhui Finance Department has stopped the lead tax on the finished case. Now, after passing through Jiangxi, this donation is levied again, which is difficult to accept. The office pointed out that tea merchants resisted the donation and blocked more than 3,000 boxes of tea from various houses, and ordered the additional payment of lead donations for box tea that had been registered before. The tea merchants had no choice but to send representatives to the Jiujiang Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association to request the general office to negotiate and release the tea. According to the report, the Xun Public Association believed that the office intended to make things difficult and sent representatives to the province to visit Director Hu of the General Office to request the cancellation of this donation and to state the suffering of tea merchants. Unexpectedly, Hu not only did not agree to the cancellation, but also pointed out that this Wuyuan box tea was produced in Dexing and must pay the donation according to regulations. The association had no choice but to telegraph the Shanghai Tea Industry Association, requesting the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to telegraph the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance to order the office to release the tea. After more than ten days, there was still no concrete solution. According to a letter from Jiujiang tea merchants yesterday, the bureau must forcibly collect this production and sales donation. The detained box tea has not been released. More than a thousand boxes of tea on the way are currently parked in Lizhou and are temporarily postponed for shipment. The two sides are in a stalemate, and it is difficult to solve it for a while. The tea industry association here believes that this illegal and harsh donation is unacceptable. Otherwise, tea exports must pass through Zhejiang and Jiangxi. If the counties follow the example of collecting donations, there will be no residue in the tea's blood. In addition to convening plenary meetings to discuss countermeasures, representatives are appointed to go to Beijing, Shanghai, Xunhan, requesting assistance from colleagues to resist until the goal is achieved. (September 9)

Jiangsu Province Business Tax 6

Cannot Be Handled Entirely Like Zhejiang

Finance Department Approves the Chamber of Commerce Federation

Zhenjiang Correspondence - The Fifth Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation had a proposal to request the Finance Department to send personnel to cooperate with the Federation to investigate and imitate Zhejiang's handling of business tax rates. It is now learned that the Finance Department has approved it, stating briefly, "According to the previous report of the Federation, the results of regional guidance and the six opinions stated have been clearly instructed. The business tax law states that the business tax rate should be determined separately by each province and city based on the nature and situation of local businesses. That is to say, the nature and situation of each province are different. Even with regard to the most important tax rate, according to the principle of tax law, each province should examine the situation and determine it separately. There is no regulation that each province must be the same. In order to take care of the difficulties of merchants, this province will postpone the implementation of the original plan to collect 10 per mille, which has been approved by the Ministry of Finance, and refer to Zhejiang's method to temporarily set three tax rates of 5 per mille, 8 per mille and 10 per mille for separate collection. In addition, the project for merchants specializing in whole sales and wholesale is allowed to be temporarily collected at half price, which is already an excessive change and a compromise. In addition, the situations in each province are different, and it is difficult to combine the methods. The request to send personnel to investigate and imitate the entire handling should not be discussed. Now that the provincial treasury is empty and military expenses are urgent, the business tax funds in each county urgently need to be collected and used. It is difficult to postpone the investigation. The Federation should immediately telegraph the local chambers of commerce and inform the merchants to comply with the regulations as soon as possible. If they continue to wait and see on the pretext, it means that they intend to obstruct. The Ministry cannot tolerate it any longer. Please comply." (September 16)

Wang Jingwei Goes to Mogan Mountain to Recuperate 7

Zhang Jingjiang and Li Shizeng Both Go to Meet and Talk

Hangzhou Correspondence: Wang Zhaoming, Standing Committee Member of the Central Political Conference and President of the Executive Yuan, suffered a relapse of an old illness. He went from Nanjing to Shanghai for medical treatment. Although special envoys from the Central Government earnestly persuaded him to return to Nanjing for treatment, his condition worsened, and his fever increased. He was temporarily unable to return to Nanjing. On the 15th, he sent separate telegrams to Ye Chucang, Secretary-General of the Central Executive Committee, and the Secretariat of the Central Political Conference, requesting an extension of his leave for two weeks and requesting that a member be entrusted to act as chairman during the meetings of the Central Political Conference, as was the custom. That night at 9:00 PM, he instructed the Railway Bureau to prepare a train, including two decorated cars and one baggage car, to depart from Shanghai's Fanwangdu to Hangzhou at 11:30 PM. In addition to Wang and his wife, Chen Bijun, there were also three secretaries and attendants. At 1:30 AM, the Hangzhou City Station received a telephone report from Shihudang Station near Fengjing, Jiashan, stating that Wang's special train had arrived at the station. The stationmaster temporarily ordered the railway police to drive away the coolies sleeping inside the station and ordered the city gates and iron gates to be closed to prevent idlers from entering or leaving. At that time, Central Committee members Chu Minyi and Zhang Fakui were waiting at the station. Newspaper reporters were also denied entry. Around 2:00 AM, the Sixth Sub-bureau of the First District received the news and sent a patrol officer to take care of the situation. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau ordered a platoon of patrol cars to rush to the station for guard duty. He Yun, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Zhong Jixing, Captain of the Patrol Brigade, also arrived at the station to welcome him. It was not until 6:30 AM on the following day (the 16th) that Wang's special train arrived at Hangzhou Station. The police force saluted with their guns. After Wang got off the train, the welcomers had prepared a hired car for Wang and his wife to ride in. However, Wang's special train already had a car of his own, so he ordered the original car to return. Immediately, Wang and his wife, secretaries, attendants, Chu, Zhang, and others, seven people in total, split into two cars and drove to Mogan Mountain to rest without stopping. At 9:20 AM, they arrived at the foot of Mogan Mountain. The management bureau had prepared sedan chairs in advance to go up the mountain. They temporarily stayed in the June Rest Garden, the villa of Zhou Xiangling, a wealthy merchant in western Zhejiang. Prominent figures staying on the mountain, such as Zhang Jingjiang and Li Shizeng, all went to visit and talked for a long time. It is said that Wang will stay for several days to recuperate. (September 16)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 8

County Hospital Opens a Morgue: The County-run Songjiang Hospital has undergone a major overhaul since appointing Dr. Zhang Shaoxiu as its director last month. The hospital wards and equipment have been newly added, and a large number of diagnostic and treatment instruments have been purchased. To facilitate childbirth, an obstetrician has been hired to oversee the obstetrics and gynecology department. The government subsidizes the regular expenses, still according to the original budget. The director has generously contributed his own funds to enrich the hospital's resources. However, the hospital still lacks a morgue, which has made it difficult to handle the aftermath of deaths. Therefore, he suggested to the authorities that this be brought up at the 21st Party-Government Meeting. It was decided that the county government should order the hospital to properly plan and set up a morgue. It is now known that the director has surveyed the buildings and estimated that the cost of installing doors and windows would be 67.30 yuan. After reporting back to the county government, the county government instructed the hospital and ordered the Finance Department to allocate 30 yuan from this year's reserve fund. The remaining shortfall will be made up by the hospital from savings in regular expenses.

Wuxi 9

Two District Chiefs Simultaneously Accused: Qian Zhongliang, the chief of the First District under the county, was recently accused by citizens Jiang, Quan, and Jinhong of being derelict in his duties, failing to publicize financial matters, and abusing his power. They submitted a petition to Sun's office, requesting that it be forwarded to the provincial government to remove him from office and appoint another competent official to manage local affairs. At the same time, citizens Deng Shuren and others from the Second District accused the district chief Zhang Guangdi of abandoning his war responsibilities and failing to publicize all public funds and income and expenditure accounts in the district for a long time, resulting in the failure to collect interest on treasury bonds. They jointly petitioned County Magistrate Chen to order an investigation and publicize the accounts in accordance with the law to protect public funds. Upon receiving the petitions, County Magistrate Chen has dispatched personnel to conduct thorough investigations in order to verify the facts and handle the matter accordingly.

New Trends in Opium Public Sales: The discussion of public opium sales has been rampant. However, the authorities believe that if they still wish to follow the previous case of establishing a smoking ban bureau and issuing licenses to smokers, it would easily provoke opposition from all parties. Currently, Jiangsu Province only allows the transport and sale of special goods from Hunan and Hubei, which is different from a complete lifting of the ban. Moreover, Jiangsu Province has not yet implemented public opium sales, so it still advocates the method of public transport and sale of domestic goods. The opinions put forward by the contractors in various counties have not been accepted. The contractors in various counties believe that this is similar to secret publicity and that the mixing of official and private goods will have a significant impact on transportation. As a result, they have all withdrawn their bids. Yin Xiangchen, the contractor from Wuxi, has returned to Wuxi from the province and has decided to give up on this special goods public sale. Those who were once rushing to bid are now disheartened and dare not ask about it. Jiangsu Province has fallen into a state of being无人问津, and in the future, the office responsible for the transport and sale of opium in Jiangsu Province, which is dispatched by the headquarters, will directly send personnel to transport and sell to various counties.

Change of Director of the Construction Bureau: Yao Dixing, the Director of the Construction Bureau of the county, was recently transferred to Yixing to replace Ge Ying, the Director of the Construction Bureau of Yixing, whose resignation was approved by the provincial government. Xiao Zicai (possibly Sicun) was appointed to act as the Director of the Construction Bureau of this county. The above order has already been issued. After receiving the order, Director Yao is currently rushing to hand over his duties. However, he has expressed his firm refusal to take up the post of Director of the Construction Bureau of Yixing. The newly appointed Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, Xiao Zicai, arrived in Wuxi from Zhenjiang by car yesterday (the 16th) with his entourage. After getting off the car, he immediately paid a visit to County Magistrate Chen and met with Director Yao. It was decided that he would take over the seal and assume his duties today (the 17th).

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Thoroughly Investigates the Excessive Issuance of Cocoon Trays: Regarding this year's autumn cocoon prices, the authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces previously convened silk cocoon leaders to discuss the standard cocoon price. It was agreed that 38 yuan would be the standard price. The autumn cocoon market in this county has been open for nearly ten days. However, due to the small amount of goods arriving, some cocoon traders have now closed their scales in order to avoid expenses. Silk manufacturers with better appetites are still excessively issuing cocoon trays and competing to purchase cocoons. Some slippery cocoon merchants with insufficient capital to turn around are also secretly issuing cocoon trays, offering five yuan per load according to the market price to lure cocoon farmers. This bad situation was learned by Tan Xihong and Zhong Kui, representatives of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in Nanjing. They sent a special telegram to the leaders of the silk cocoon industry in this county, Qian Fenghao and Hua Shaochun, requesting them to earnestly persuade their colleagues to maintain the provincial government's principle of standard cocoon prices and to investigate the initiator of the destruction for investigation. The original telegram stated: "To Qian Fenghao, Chairman of the Wuxi Silk Factory Association, and Hua Shaochun, Chairman of the Cocoon Industry Association: It has been reported that the cocoon price in Wuxi is being competitively raised to 60 yuan, which is extremely alarming. The government's relief of the silk industry originally aimed for the silk industry to work together to restore its original position. Currently, the silk market has slightly improved, but colleagues are deceiving each other and disregarding everything. This is tantamount to running counter to the government's intentions. We urge your association to earnestly persuade your colleagues to strive to maintain the provincial government's principle of standard cocoon prices and to investigate the initiator of the excessive issuance for investigation."

A Passenger on the Longda Steamer Was Beaten to Death by the Tea Room: On the 7th of this month, when the Longda Steamer of the Shanghai-Yangzhou Datong Company arrived at Ren Port, the ticket inspector found that a passenger, Mr. A, had not purchased a ticket. It is said that the amount should be shared equally by the education directors and cabinet secretaries who have served in the past five years. It is reported that the 7,000 yuan of the director's share has been collected separately by the cabinet secretaries and remitted to the county. As for the half that the cabinet secretaries themselves should return, they repeatedly requested the county magistrate to request the Provincial Department of Education to allow them to postpone the payment. County Magistrate Yang was afraid that the collection would be too urgent and would affect the current revenue of money and grain, so he reported the situation to the Provincial Department and asked for help. It is said that the Provincial Department of Education expressed deep dissatisfaction with the request for a temporary postponement. It immediately ordered the county government to still follow the previous orders and instruct them to pay within the specified time. If they set up excuses to disobey again, they will be escorted to the province for pressing.

Nantong 12

Strict Prohibition Along the Coast of Nantong: Due to the recent discovery of more than 1,000 bandits in the coastal areas of Tongshu Kenmu Sanyu near the town of the company, most of them carrying firearms, the situation is very rampant. The fields are temporarily under martial law. The county government received a report on the 15th and transferred a police force to be stationed.

Registration for Public Sale of Opium: After the implementation of public transport of opium in Tongyi, public sales are now being carried out. Xu, a Guangbang member, is acting as the contractor. Local urban and rural vendors must register first, and each household will be charged 100 yuan.

Deadline for Handing Over Overflowed滩田: Xu Xiaoxian, a famous shagun in Tongyi, was arrested by the county government upon provincial order and given a deadline to hand over 500 mu of overflowed Liuhai sha滩田. The sha滩田 will be discounted by the provincial government at 60 yuan per mu and given to the Nantong Education Bureau to receive, and the money will be sent to the provincial treasury.

It took an hour to extinguish the fire. After investigation, it was found that a total of 17 shops of various sizes were burned, with losses of approximately 20,000 yuan.

Opening of Zhejiang Provincial Library 17

A Memorial Day in the History of Chinese Culture

The Zhejiang Provincial Library, with a collection of 250,000 books, is one of the largest libraries in the country. It also houses the Wenlan Pavilion Siku Quanshu, which has become a national rare book. Therefore, it occupies a special position in the national culture. The new main building on Daxue Road was completed and relocated the day before yesterday (the 15th), and an opening ceremony was held. That day happened to be the 100th anniversary of the birth of Mr. Ding Songshan, who supplemented and transcribed the Wenlan Pavilion Siku Quanshu. The library has specially opened a room to display the documents and manuscripts left by Mr. Ding to remember the sages and inspire future generations. That day is indeed worthy of leaving a memorial in cultural history.

The New Anhui Education Director Will Take Office 18

Arriving in Anhui Around the 20th of This Month

The new Anhui Education Director, Zhu Tinghu, recently sent a telegram to the Ministry of Education, stating that he has replied to Chairman Wu of Anhui Province that he will arrive in Anhui around the 20th, and is hereby informing you.

University and College 19

Cancellation of the Examination of Party Training Teachers

The Ministry of Education issued a notice to all colleges and universities above the specialized level regarding the cancellation of the examination of Party Ideology teachers and deans of student affairs in universities and colleges, stating: "The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang's Office in Beijing approved a public letter No. 10236, stating: 'The Central Committee's 35th Standing Committee, according to a report from the Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee, stated that the examination of Party Ideology teachers and deans of student affairs in universities and colleges was originally intended to carefully select personnel to promote the development of Party Ideology education. Later, due to overly strict regulations, the examination was changed to a review, and it has not been successful for more than a year. Now that the Ministry of Education is studying the cancellation of the independent status of Party Ideology courses in colleges and universities above the specialized level in detail, it seems that there is no need to continue reviewing Party Ideology teachers and deans of student affairs in universities and colleges. Therefore, the 10th meeting decided to cancel the review of the qualifications of Party Ideology teachers in universities and colleges, and all documents and certificates of personnel requesting review stored by the Central Party Ideology Teacher Qualification Review Committee will be returned. Is this appropriate? Please make a public decision, etc.' The decision has been passed and is being sent to you for reference."

Local

Municipal Bureau of Education 20

Calling Principals of Primary and Secondary Schools for Talks

Reporting Three Matters

Since taking office, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, has been actively planning and promoting the city's education, sparing no effort. Yesterday, he specially called the principals of primary and secondary schools in the city for talks. Director Pan reported three matters, hoping that primary and secondary schools will pay attention to them: (1) Regarding the September 18th National Humiliation Memorial Day, the Ministry of Education has issued a clear order that schools should hold memorial meetings on that day to talk about the facts of national humiliation and arouse students' self-motivation. Avoid going out for parades to avoid accidents. (2) The failure of university education in the past was not due to a single reason, but the lack of strict training for students in secondary schools was the biggest reason. It is hoped that the principals of each school will adopt strict principles in training students to establish a foundation for university education. (3) Although the city's education funds are still fixed at 1.2 million per year, it is feared that they cannot be received in full due to the city's financial difficulties. It is hoped that each school will adopt a tight policy and save on various expenses to avoid being caught off guard when financial difficulties arise. Personally, I am deeply concerned about my downfall in assuming this position during this time of national crisis. If you have any suggestions, please let me know at any time, and I will adopt them sincerely.

Chairman Lin Visited Liu Haisu the Other Day 21

After Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government came to Shanghai the other day, he specially took a car to the Fine Arts School to visit Mr. Liu Haisu on the afternoon of the 12th amidst his busy government affairs. Mr. Liu happened to be at the Liu Shi Exhibition of the Chinese Art Society. Mr. Lin followed him to the Art Society. Mr. Liu Haisu cordially invited him to visit his nephew's exhibition. Chairman Lin advocated promoting art and learning to save the Jieyun. He plans to build an art museum in the capital. On the one hand, he urged Mr. Liu to go to Luoyang to collect antiquities in advance, so that they can be used as part of the museum's collection in the future. He also inquired in detail about Mr. Liu's art exhibition in Germany. The chairman paid great attention to this matter, believing that it was of great importance to international culture. The chairman has long supported Mr. Liu's works, often saying that Chinese art has been trapped in a long-term stagnation. Now Mr. Liu 　　　 is breaking out a bloody path. His courage to win is naturally well-received. On the same day, Mr. Liu painted a portrait of the chairman, which will be displayed in the exhibition.

Fudan Moved Back to the Original Site in Jiangwan to Start Classes 22

After being ravaged by the Japanese army after the January 28th Incident, Fudan University in Jiangwan has recently been cleaned up. On September 7, 8, and 9, it moved back to its original site in Jiangwan. The Shanghai News reporter specially visited the school yesterday morning to inquire about everything. He was received by Mr. Jin Tongyin, the secretary-general of the school, who said that due to financial reasons, the scope of the courses in each department this semester will be reduced and the content will be enriched. However, courses such as Northeast Studies, Japanese Studies, and Manchurian Studies have been added. The professors of each department have been hired. The newly hired professors of the Faculty of Arts include Xie Hairuo and Yuan Daofeng. The newly hired professors of the Department of Political Science of the Faculty of Law include Geng Zuojun, Yuan Daonong, and Fei Gong. The newly hired professors of the Department of Law include Zhong Hongsheng, Yu Chengxiu, Qu Cengze, Hu Han　, Jiang Zhensan, Shi Lin, and Jin Lansun. Registration will begin on the 19th of this month, and classes will officially begin on the 21st.

It is also reported that the Fudan Experimental High School has also moved back to its original site in Jiangwan, and the Junior High School is located at 55 Kangnaidao Road. A large number of new books, instruments, and specimens have been purchased, and Chen Yimin, who returned from France, has been newly hired as a physics and chemistry professor, as well as Guo Xueshi, Zhen Yan, Yu Kangjunwei, and other teachers.

Yesterday, the Olympic Delegation 25

Shen Siliang and Others Arrived in Shanghai

Shen Talks About the International Impression of This Trip Is Very Good

Welcomed Everywhere, Regardless of Success or Failure

Song Junfu and Liu Changchun Head North This Morning

Shen Siliang (General Representative), Song Junfu (Coach), and Liu Changchun (Athlete), members of the Chinese delegation attending the 10th World Games, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 8:30 AM on the President Coolidge. They landed at the New Customs Wharf. Those who came to welcome them included relatives and friends of each person, as well as people from the sports and news circles. Mr. Shen had a lot of luggage, and the inspection took time. It was not until 11:00 AM that he left the port and went to the University of John. Song and Liu went to the Qingjian Association in Baxianqiao by car at 9:30 AM to stay. This morning at 9:30 AM, they took the Beijing-Shanghai train to Beijing and then took the Pingpu train north. Mr. Tuoping, director of the West Qing Sports Department, also came to Shanghai on the same ship. The details are recorded below.

Shen's Speech

Welcomed Everywhere: In the United States, in addition to the enthusiastic welcome from the Chinese community, the American people also showed goodwill to us everywhere, regardless of success or failure. Mr. Tuoping of the Shanghai Western Qingnian Association interacted with us every day to connect feelings. Therefore, although China's participation in this conference was small and there were no achievements, it did gain a sense of national sympathy and an excellent impression in the international community.

The Process of Attending the Conference: We left Shanghai on July 8 to participate in the 10th World Games, and arrived in Los Angeles late at night on the 29th. When we arrived at the pier, dozens of overseas Chinese stood to welcome us, which greatly increased our happiness. The next day, we went to the conference for the opening ceremony. On the second day of the conference, Mr. Liu Changchun began to compete. Although he did not win a medal, Mr. Liu's spirit of struggle is commendable, and he has gained a lot of experience. Therefore, it is only necessary to contribute personal experience and promote it. Conduct precise discussions in preparation for participating again in the future. I firmly believe that if the government and the people can cooperate, have a thorough understanding of this, vigorously promote it, make a final decision, and continuously carry it out, strive for universality, then it will not be difficult to compare with Europe and the United States in four years.

Results of the Conference: The conference closed on August 14. The United States won the first place with 41 medals, followed by Italy, France, and Sweden. We set off on the 21st and were able to meet with the compatriots in Shanghai today. He also said that all the experiences along the way to the United States have been repeatedly recorded in newspapers. There were no special incidents when returning to Shanghai.

心怵目: When the ship arrived at Kobe, we did not go ashore. It is said that before Japan recognized the fake Manchuria, there were celebrations every day. There were slogans and publicity everywhere on the streets. All entertainment venues, etc., had signs with the words "September 18th National Day Celebration Day, free admission."

Liu's Speech

Feeling Very Sorry: The reporter went to the Youth Association at 3:00 PM to visit Mr. Liu Changchun. Here is a record of his speech: I (Liu calls himself below this imitation) went to the United States to participate in the 10th World Games. I did not prepare beforehand, so I did not achieve any results. I am ashamed of the country and hope that the people of the country will forgive me. At the same time, I hope to work hard and prepare for the next大会, which will be held in 1936. As for my participation this time, it was not dispatched by the government. All the travel expenses, a total of more than 8,000 yuan, were all provided by private individuals. Therefore, I only represent the people of China.

Safe Voyage: We set off from Los Angeles on August 21 and returned to the country on the President Coolidge from San Francisco on the 26th. Those traveling with us included Mr. Tuoping, the executive director of the sports department of the Shanghai Western Overseas Youth Association, and Tishang, etc. I still have to stay in the car for more than a month before I can return to the country. The voyage was very safe. The sea was calm and quiet all the way, without the suffering of颠簸.

American Welcome: When we were in the United States, the American people showed us a warm welcome everywhere and took great care of us. Even after I failed in the competition, they all came to shake hands, as if to express their regret for me. They were very cold to the Japanese players. Japan showed a mocking attitude everywhere. Even the spectators in the Games, when they saw Japanese players falling or failing, unanimously let out a kind of mocking sound. Only the Japanese players had thick skin and always tried their best to do it.

Heading North This Morning: Mr. Yu and Mr. Song (Junfu) were originally scheduled to go to Peiping on the 18th, but Mr. Song's home was suddenly looted by bandits, so they had no intention to stay any longer. They decided to take the early train from Shanghai to Beijing this morning and transfer to the Pingpu train to go north. All the entertainments in Shanghai were declined.

Olympic Games 27

A Glimpse of the Closing Ceremony (Shen Siliang)

The grandness of the World Games closing ceremony matched the opening ceremony from start to finish. After two weeks of the world's gathering here, it temporarily came to an end. Everyone felt sorrow at the prospect of leaving such a solemn and stimulating event, and their emotions were clearly visible. Moved by the scene, each carried their own sorrow, even to the point of sobbing and weeping. Strong heroes displaying childlike emotions at this time and in this scene will be forever unforgettable to us.

Flag Ceremony After the final sporting event (equestrian jumping competition) in the stadium, all the equipment was removed. A 500-member military band and a 2,000-person choir entered the field and played again. Then, officials carrying national flags and the Olympic flag paraded in formation, similar to the opening ceremony. Because some athletes had already returned to their home countries, they did not participate. After the procession, the flags gathered in front of the podium, forming a semicircle called the "Flag Ceremony."

Speeches The closing ceremony included speeches by the following individuals. Their words were concise but very sincere: (1) Count de Balle Latour, President of the Olympic Committee; (2) Mayor Portor of Los Angeles; (3) Chairman Garland of the American Organizing Committee; (4) President of the German Amateur Sports Association (as the 11th Games were scheduled to be held in Germany).

Flag Presentation The organizing committee specially prepared an embroidered flag to be presented to the organizing committee of the host city as a gesture of gratitude and a symbol of honor. The flag was specially made and presented by the Mayor of Amsterdam, having been kept in the Amsterdam City Hall for four years. This time, the Mayor personally came to the Games to transfer the flag to the Mayor of Los Angeles, to be kept in the Los Angeles City Hall until the 1936 Games, when the flag will be sent to Berlin.

Cannon Fire When all stood in solemn silence until the end of the speeches, the Olympic emblem (interlocking rings of different colors) was lowered, and the torch that had been burning for sixteen days and nights was extinguished. At the same time, cannons fired and horns sounded. The flags of the United States, Germany, and the Netherlands were raised on the high tower, signifying the intent of these nations to host the 9th, 10th and 11th games.

Finale After the choir sang "Aloha - Till We Meet Again," the national flags and emblems were withdrawn from the grandstand, gradually disappearing from sight. The Olympic flag was carried by eight people to the center of the field, and as the song ended, the flag was rolled up, marking the end of the grand sporting event. (Reports from the Olympic Village and the press box will be published tomorrow.)

Chicago Night Games 33

5,000 Meter Race

Still Cannot Resolve Olympic Doubts

Hill Fails, Ritola Does Not Finish

World Male and Female Stars Participate in Performances

Chicago, August 18th dispatch. The question of who was the 5,000-meter champion at the World Games, with the Americans claiming Finland's Ritola deliberately obstructed America's Hill, remains unresolved. Therefore, a sporting event was held in Chicago on the night of the 18th to resolve the question. As a result, neither Ritola, the official Olympic champion, nor Hill won. The Olympic 10,000-meter champion, Poland's Kusocinski, took first place.

(1) Finland's Ritola Drops Out Mid-Race. The entire stadium was illuminated with electric lights, as bright as day. "Special Publication" The Olympic Games After-Meeting." More than 35,000 spectators. Ritola, the Finnish general whom the Olympic referees considered the champion, dropped out mid-race. Hill was left behind by Kusocinski and was no match. Although Hill made a great effort in the final lap, Ritola said he withdrew because of an ankle injury, having run 2,800 meters in 14 minutes and 59.9 seconds, slower than Hill's Olympic time.

(2) A Grand Gathering of Olympic Stars. In addition, male and female athletes from this year's Olympics performed, with the following results:

Poland's Walasiewicz (1) 100 meters in 11.9 seconds, matching her own world record; (2) 200 meters in 24.1 seconds, a new record.

American Didrikson (1) High jump, first place with a height of 5 feet 2 inches; (2) Discus, 133 feet. (Didrikson set world records in the women's javelin and low hurdles at this year's Games.)

Poland's Wasana, Discus, first place 137 feet 3 and 3/4 inches.

American Sexton, Olympic shot put champion, this evening's shot put result was 51 feet 1 and 1/4 inches.

American Miller, Olympic pole vault champion, tied for first with Grabner, who took third place at the Olympics, with a height of 13 feet 9 inches, short of Miller's own world record.

American Metcalfe, 100 meters first place, 10.3 seconds, matching the world record. German Borchmeyer, 200 meters first place, 21.2 seconds, matching Tolan's Olympic record.

Commercial News

Financial Swap, Gold Market Momentum 34

Shorts Post Up to Twelve Taels The price of gold suddenly soared yesterday. Coinciding with the gold exchange's scheduled swap day, business began an hour earlier at 8:00 AM, as per regulations. However, gold firms had already been trading outside the exchange in the early morning. The October-to-November swap was still posted by the shorts, initially at 6 taels and 5 mace, then 7 taels and 5 mace, with the lowest at 6 taels. When formally listed, it was 11 taels, as most longs were unwilling to swap lightly, while the shorts, being in the majority, were eager to swap in, causing the price to rise to 12 taels. It then rallied again, closing in the morning at 9 taels and 7 mace. Hengxing swapped long, while the shorts had already swapped properly. All October contracts were untraded. Opening volume was 729 taels, closing in the morning at 36.5 taels, up 14 taels and 8 mace from the 14th. This was due to the November listing being transferred. In the afternoon, the listing was canceled as usual, and most switched to trading November contracts.

November Contract Market Extremely Sharp The November contract was listed yesterday, and the situation was extremely sharp and the trend was smooth. It was particularly high at midday, with a difference of 10 taels between the morning and midday. However, the spread was only about 4 taels at most. Demand from fellow traders was very strong and bullish. The reason for the sharp rise was due to the large bullion price increase, American silver parity, and the fall in forwards and exchange rates, further exacerbated by the large swap. It was firm from the morning, mainly due to the tight foreign exchange situation, so progress was very rapid, continuing to rise by 10 taels. Later in the market, there was also a reversal of about 5 taels. Initially, it was strong and sharp, foreign exchange frequently contracted, and then it seemed to turn loose. As many longs sold off, the price fell sharply by more than 4 taels, finally closing between 724 taels, about 12 taels higher than before the closure (14th) (excluding the swap). Overall, bullion demand was still short. Here is a detailed account of the day's situation.

Morning Market Progresses Rapidly The November contract opened early at 718 taels, followed by 17 taels and 8 mace. The large bullion price had risen by one-quarter over the past two days, American silver rose and then fell, reaching parity, and silver futures repeatedly fell by 1.5 cents, so sentiment immediately rose. Shortly after, there was a 2 tael spread. At 8:30, buyers were active, with Qian Changxiang, Hengxing, Yuan Yifeng, Yongtong, Taichang, etc. all buying in, and the price rose by 4 taels. At 9:15, it was 22 taels and 3 mace, due to Yuan Kangxiang, Yuantai, Hengxing, and Yonglai selling and American dollars for October at 81.25 being available for settlement, and Zhongfu selling December at 31.0625, so at 9:30 it was 20 taels and 3 mace. HSBC listed English level American contracted 125, when the gold price was still level, around 21 taels. Hengxing sold out, retreating to around 20 taels. Then, Hengyu, Dadecheng, Yuanheng, Zhaofengchang, Zhifeng, and Yong bought in, and American dollars for December was doing 31 yuan, so the gold price rose by 3 taels until 10:15, when it was 23 taels and 5 mace. Later, because Huabi, etc. sold December at 31 yuan, Yuan Kangxiang, Yuantai, Futaiheng, Bingxing, etc. sold out, it ceded 2 taels. However, the up and down did not reach 1 tael until 11:00, when it was 21 taels and 5 mace. In the later market, the situation felt even sharper, and American dollars for December at 31 yuan could be sold to settle at .875, demand was very strong, and on the table, Xie Xing, Yong Richang, Yifeng, Yong Bingxing, Qian Changxiang, etc. were all buying in, a jump of three or four taels. It was particularly strong at 11:45, as it was known that the Prime Minister was expected to be reduced. Hengxing, Yuan Dadecheng, Fuyu, Hengyu, Fuchang, Yuanxing, Yong, etc. worked hard to buy in, so it was again stimulated by three taels all the way forward to 27 taels and 8 mace at 11:50. Then, Hengyu Zhaofengchang, etc. spat it out, and ceded 1 tael, and American dollars for December could be settled at .9375, until the market closed at 26 taels and 8 mace, and HSBC listed the fruit shrink 125, American dollars shrink 125, but did not take it as movement, it was already done early.

Afternoon Market Sharpness Slightly Restrained The afternoon market opened at 26 taels and a half, followed by 8 taels and 1 mace, Yifeng Yong·Qian Changxiang sold out, and Huabi sold October American dollars at 30 and a half yuan, followed by zero households also selling out, so it was 26 taels and 7 mace. At the moment, Dadecheng, etc. bought in, and they knew that the Prime Minister had been reduced for the second time by 125, and the American dollars by 25, so they immediately added more than 1 tael, for 28 taels and 4 mace. After that, it was indeed hung shrunk, but it had already released its gas, and Yifeng Yong·Bingxing·Fuchang·Zhaofengchang were all out, HSBC came out with October American dollars at half a yuan, December at 75, at 2:30 for 26 taels and 6 mace. After entering, Mitsui absorbed January .875, and did half a yuan for October, Zhifeng Yong bought in, and added 1 tael, at 3:20 for 27 taels and 7 mace, but in these three quarters of an hour there were only a few cents up and down. Flour: Sharp Decline and Small Rebound 43

Yesterday, the flour market showed signs of a sharp decline after opening in the morning. The prices for foreign wheat plummeted by 0.5-0.7 taels from the closing price before the market break. Although the price rebounded by 0.1-0.3 taels yesterday, the near-term outlook remained poor. Therefore, market sentiment was weak after the opening. Later, foreign firms reportedly dumped wheat at extremely low prices, with rumors of 3.75 taels being offered and even 3.72 taels being considered, causing market panic. Sellers aggressively sold, and mill outputs were strong. The momentum of selling and the rumors of foreign wheat dumping caused long-term contracts to decline even more. The strange phenomenon of November contracts being inverted was seen, showing market sentiment was bleak. At the close, the trading volume reached over 600,000, with prices falling by 0.2-0.4 taels. When the market opened in the afternoon, market sentiment gradually stabilized, and mills stopped selling. Some speculative positions were covered, and market sentiment improved slightly, rebounding by about 0.1 taels. However, the practice of ordering foreign wheat has begun, and prices are unlikely to rise excessively. As a result, this month's price fell by 0.0125 taels compared to before the market break, October fell by 0.0175 taels, November fell by 0.0225 taels, December fell by 0.0275 taels, and January and February each fell by 0.03 taels.

Wheat Futures Show Signs of Weakening 44

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed signs of stabilization in the morning for all months. When the market opened in the afternoon, market sentiment weakened again due to the sharp decline in the flour market in the morning and the negative sentiment regarding foreign wheat. Free Talk

Two One-Branch Talks

Slogans Are Not as Good as Heartfelt Calls 50

— Zhanlu

The gun barrel should be pointed outward. We, who shout slogans, should not focus solely on shouting loudly to the outside world but should emphasize internal action to awaken our unpolluted conscience!

Solely shouting slogans to the outside world, you shout a sentence, and others echo you with the same sentence. If it's good, it's called awakening the national soul. If it's bad, it's like the frog teaching in "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio" or the "humming" of the Xiangshan artisans, or the chanting of sutras by the storytelling master.

In ancient times, when facing national and familial shame, people instructed others to shout slogans at themselves, not themselves shouting slogans at the masses. King Fuchai of Wu was a model example. To avenge the murder of his father by the King of Yue, he instructed someone to stand in the courtyard and loudly proclaim to him: "Fuchai! Have you forgotten the King of Yue who killed your father?"

In ancient times, people also spurred themselves on by shouting slogans to themselves! This slogan was not shouted aloud but recited silently. Zengzi was a model example. He examined himself three times a day, reciting the slogans silently to himself each day, calling out: "Have I been disloyal in my efforts for others? Have I been untrustworthy in my dealings with friends? Have I not practiced what I have been taught?" Slogans are not as good as heartfelt calls. Zengzi's method of self-鞭策 is more measured than Fuchai's. The anniversary of September 18th has arrived. I hope everyone adopts Zengzi's method of heartfelt calls, examining themselves three times a day, silently encouraging their own inner action to save the country.

Shouting slogans at meetings is certainly indispensable! My point is that heartfelt calls are more important than slogans. Those who have shouted slogans at meetings should especially examine themselves three times a day, silently calling out with their hearts.

Shanghai Miss 51

— Baishi

People in Shanghai call girls "Miss." The term "Miss" is not particularly rare. Girl, maiden, lass, young woman are all similar terms, used according to local customs. But adding "Shanghai" before "Miss" makes a big difference. "Shanghai Miss" does not mean any Miss who lives in Shanghai. The formation of a Shanghai Miss has conditions. Now I will explain the conditions for forming a Shanghai Miss.

When a Shanghai Miss is born, she is no different from others, like the ancient sages. But when she is around ten years old, if her parents intend for her to become a Shanghai Miss, then they must send her to a aristocratic school. The purpose of going to such schools is not about grades, curriculum, etc. First, it is to make the daughter understand what is called "beauty" and how "beauty" is cultivated. After class, she should not be allowed to do housework, because cooking, washing, wiping tables, and sweeping floors are fundamentally destructive to "beauty." The only work after class is to practice singing and dancing, because singing is practice for the vocal organs, and dancing can make muscles develop evenly and increase the curves. In addition, eating chocolate, spearmint gum, soda, and ice cream are also very important. Because this kind of training of the stomach is also very beneficial for future social prospects. From elementary school to middle school, all the way to university graduation, training in this unchanging way, plus some courses on watching movies, eating fancy meals, and riding in cars, will naturally create a generous, up-to-date, healthy, and beautiful social star, or in other words, a flower of society, or in other words, a Shanghai Miss.

The formation of a Shanghai Miss is not an easy thing. Without a wealthy father and a noble environment, don't think about becoming a Shanghai Miss. Some people who have not been properly trained and desperately try to become Shanghai Misses are truly miserable.

Two Youths on the Sea 52

— Ti Gong

The two youths I know are both from wealthy families, enjoying the benefits of their ancestors. However, their actions are like ice and charcoal. Youth A, after the death of his parents, observes a vegetarian diet and worships Buddha. His home is always full of monks and Taoists, and he only hopes for his parents' rebirth in the Western Paradise, free from the suffering of reincarnation. Six years have passed like one day. He wears plain clothes and cloth shoes, and treats people with courtesy. No one would recognize him as the wealthy son of a mansion who rides a motorcycle. Youth B spends nights indulging in pleasure, squandering money like dirt. His father divided the family property for him, but he squandered it all in over a year and still demanded money relentlessly. If the old man even slightly offended him, he would raise his arms and threaten him, saying, "Killing you is nothing more than paying with my life." His attitude was fierce, like the impetuous and bold Zhang Xinsheng. The old man could only swallow his voice and weep, letting him do as he pleased, even afraid to show any anger. The world is full of people like Yang Wanshi, but I have never heard of anyone being afraid of their son like this. It also awaits Ma Jie Fu to come forward and lend a hand.

Who is Youth B? I don't want to say. Youth A is the so-called Lonely Lotus Hermit on the sea.

Taking Words Literally 53

— Yiwei Sheng

| Correcting a few misunderstandings |

Each character in our country's writing has its own meaning. Although many words need to combine several characters to create a new meaning, especially transliterations and direct translations of foreign words, because people have deeply ingrained the concept that each character has its own meaning, they still inevitably interpret these foreign words character by character, leading to many jokes or misunderstandings. For example, when copper coins were first circulated in Guangdong, because there was no corresponding customary name and because Hong Kong copper coins had already been introduced, the English word "CENTS" was transliterated as "仙士" (xian shi, meaning "immortal scholar"). However, some superstitious people believed that calling copper coins that would profane "仙" (xian, immortal) and "士" (shi, scholar), especially the inviolability of "仙," so they euphemistically called them "大錢" (da qian, big money) or "鏍" (luo, screw). This "鏍" character is pronounced like the level tone of the word "累" (lei, tired). In our childhood, this alternative name for copper coins was very common. Even now, people in Guangdong villages still call them that. Another example is the recently popular term "模特兒" (mote'er), which is a transliteration of the English word "MODEL." The original meaning is a model or exemplar, so people who pose for paintings are also called "模特兒." In fact, if you use a dog or a cow as a model for painting, you can also call it a "模特兒." However, in a society that takes words literally, because this term has the character "兒" (er, son) at the end and because of nude female figure painting, they have rigidly defined "模特兒" as a special term for nude women and even consider "模特兒" as an obscene and shameful term. This is truly a joke. Another example is "幽默" (youmo), which is also transliterated from the English word "HUMOUR." The original meaning is "humorous" and thought-provoking, similar to "滑稽" (huaji, comical). However, the person who coined the term thought that "滑稽" had been used excessively and even had a vulgar and frivolous connotation, so he did not translate Humour as "滑稽" but translated it as "幽默" instead. In fact, "幽默" is not a bad translation, but these two characters are too meaningful, because these two characters happen to be adjectives, and the meanings of the two characters are very similar. So, those who take words literally misunderstand them again. Misunderstanding is not a big deal, but they actually misuse them. They use "幽默" as "靜默" (jingmo, silent) or "幽靜" (youjing, tranquil). This is another big joke! If they see the recently popular terms "法西斯蒂" (faxisidi, fascist) or "布爾喬亞" (buerqiaoa, bourgeoisie), I wonder what they will think!

A Poem for Palanquin Carriers 54

— Shiyu

| Self-Reliance | And Self-Striving

In the past, when I was a teacher, I often told my students that self-reliance is the purest and most noble thing. For example, the money earned by those who sell pancakes and those who pull rickshaws is more worthy than the salaries of those in various government offices, agencies, and bureaus who can actually do their jobs without shame. Even we teachers sometimes catch a cold and miss a class or two, but we still receive our salaries without deduction. We should feel ashamed of those who labor. Therefore, I say that labor is sacred. Because pancake sellers cannot miss making even half a pancake, and rickshaw pullers cannot walk fewer than ten or eight steps, the money they earn is truly earned and they have no reason to be ashamed. I went to Mogan Mountain this time and after admiring the Biwu Waterfall, I was moved by the palanquin carriers' ability to work hard and strive. I wrote a poem for them:

Returning from viewing the waterfall, my feet are already weary,

Riding in a mountain palanquin, following the mountain's turns.

From high to low and low to high,

Contorted, wanting to look up, quickly bowing.

Mountain rocks are rugged, the path is narrow and dangerous,

The palanquin carriers all pant like Wu oxen.

Ten miles of road, a hundred miles of difficulty,

Straw sandals torn, one foot bare.

Sweat drips drop by drop onto the grass roots,

Mountain grass grows lusher, the ground richer.

Passing a ruined temple, briefly stopping the palanquin,

To drink clear spring water, seeking shade to rest.

Breath not yet steady, they set off again,

Commendable for their labor, self-striving and encouraging.

With this spirit and strength, they can handle great affairs,

Virtue and kindness widely spread, their plans and strategies unfolding.

How few are those who are wealthy and noble who cannot be corrupted,

Their spirit and strength fully revealed, their ugliness hidden.

Great are the palanquin carriers, my teachers,

Each step on solid ground, without shame.

Novelist's Rotary Club: Silver Threads (16) 55

— Jiang Hongjiao

(8)

"I don't know what other people there are besides you, except for my country, my hometown. I shed blood for you, and I am willing to sacrifice everything for you. I was not wounded on the battlefield, but I have suffered a great wound in my heart, which no one can heal except you. I am willing to give my life to the entire Chinese nation and do not want to receive any honors, but at least from you, I want to regain the rights to love that I lost before; because at that time I was not a soldier, so a soldier—your husband—snatched you away. I know that you admire warriors, and brave warriors, so I desperately resisted foreign aggression. I don't want to think about the future, I just want to continue to adhere to your principles and continue my work."

"I still don't understand how you only found me now. What happened before?"

"The day before yesterday, Zhu Qibo's daughter came to see me in the city. She came quietly alone. Her purpose was to express her sincere love to me, to make me understand that it is a very normal thing for a girl to admire a hero and be willing to show her love to him; but the people of the whole town, persuaded by her, unanimously worshiped a hero and donated money, which is extremely difficult. She also told me that there was a crazy woman and a poor widow in the town who had both donated money, which was very touching. I told her that I already had a very beautiful, intelligent, and affectionate wife, and that I was very satisfied and would soon introduce her to the people in the town. Sacrificing for the country is the responsibility of every citizen and should not be regarded as a particularly glorious thing, so it would be best to cancel the monument construction."

"Then how did you know that this poor widow was me, and that I lived here?"

"She also said that this was your modesty. You have contributed to the country, and both women and children admire you, which is truly worthy of praise! Like this widow, who lives a very hard life herself and also supports an unrelated crazy woman, yet she also managed to contribute a sum, isn't that your heroic honor? She repeatedly praised this widow, so I asked her what her name was and where she lived. She told me everything, and she was willing to take me to see this widow on the day of the dedication ceremony, so I kept it in my heart and was surprised and grateful to this Miss Zhu. I heard that she kissed me before we parted, so I agreed to personally attend the dedication ceremony."

"She kissed you?"

"Yes, she kissed my hand deeply."

"Then you should be happy. Someone is building a monument for you, someone is giving you a kiss. You should be satisfied!"

"But you won't let me heal the wound in my heart."

"I heard that it is this Miss Zhu who will be in charge of the unveiling ceremony today. You should go to the meeting soon, to avoid her deep anticipation and unease."

"It is very easy for a soldier to have several women to comfort him, but there is no one who can understand the soldier's heart; especially me, I do not need flattery like meat on a chopping board, but I crave the spirit of a woman's pure soul."

They disembarked at the China Merchants Zhongzhan Pier and went straight to their private residence to rest. The content roughly said that a war between Japan and the United States must have a flashpoint in a certain place in China. After the start of the war, the Japanese navy can occupy the Philippines within three days, and Honolulu is also in danger. Therefore, the U.S. government cannot have any positive expression unless it has obtained diplomatic support. As for a war between Japan and Russia, although it is relatively more possible, the current Soviet Russia is making every effort to consolidate its internal affairs and make its social economy tend to stability. It adopts an extremely tolerant doctrine toward external oppression. Even its external propaganda of communism has recently reduced its strength. Therefore, even with various provocations from the Japanese side, Russia is retreating step by step and will never have a head-on collision, which can also be asserted, etc.

National Salvation Through Self-Salvation: Mr. Wu also said that since the League of Nations is incapable and a war between Japan and the United States or Japan and Russia is impossible, will our people just sit idly by and watch the loss of the three northeastern provinces and be helpless? No. National salvation can only be achieved through self-salvation. On the one hand, the volunteer armies in various parts of the Northeast are making continuous resistance in difficult circumstances. On the other hand, the people are strictly implementing economic severance. Then, although Japan has obtained the Northeast, the expenditure on military expenses is huge. At the same time, due to the disturbance of the volunteer army, it affects its production volume. At that time, its country will definitely feel the pain of not being worth the loss. Our country can take the opportunity to use diplomacy, or it can manipulate the final victory.

Not to Serve as a Diplomat: The reporter also asked if the central government intends to rely on you to take charge of diplomatic affairs, what would you express? Mr. Wu replied that I plan to go north by waterway this time and will not go to Nanjing for the time being. Even if the central government has this intention, I will definitely not dare to accept the order because of my weak talent. Doing diplomacy requires internal unity, otherwise, the opinions of the government and the people will be divided, and the people in the government will act on their own. Then what can be done externally, etc. Mr. Wu also said that Mr. Sun Zhesheng will come to Shanghai soon and will be the head of the Executive Yuan. I have not heard of it before. As for Mr. Hu Zhantang, he has no intention of coming to Shanghai for the time being.

Willing to Return to Lead Qiongyai: Regarding the position of the head of the Qiongyai Special Zone, Mr. Wu said that he has never resigned from it. However, now that the Qiongyai area is not peaceful, he is still willing to go to take office after it is pacified, etc.
