Due to Inspection of Opium 60

The Jiangshun Steamer Caused a Misunderstanding by a Japanese Warship

Almost Leading to a Major Dispute

On the night of the 14th, the Jiangshun Steamer fired a pistol due to the Water Patrol's inspection of opium, which caused a misunderstanding by a Japanese warship, which sent troops to search the ship. After obstruction by the ship's crew, it stopped. The steamer left port yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

Opium Inspection Dispute: The Jiangshun Steamer, which arrived in Shanghai from Hankou this time, was docked at the Nanzhan Pier after entering the port. At around 8:00 PM on the afternoon of the 14th, several water patrol team leaders and police officers came to the ship to search for opium. After searching everywhere, they found nothing. The water police then went to the fire room and questioned the ship's stoker, Qian Caiyun, harshly, ordering him to hand it over. Qian refused, and a conflict occurred. The water police then locked up three stokers in the fire room and questioned them severely, which also sparked a dispute. They beat each other, and three stokers were injured.

Firing Empty Shots: After this incident occurred, the ship's chief engineer, G. Goulton, was informed and rushed into the fire room. Seeing that four of the sailors had been injured, he argued with the water police. The water police also bruised his leg. He then left the cabin and went to the deck. At that time, the water police drew his pistol and fired six or seven shots into the air, unexpectedly causing a misunderstanding by the Japanese navy, which almost led to a major accident.

Japanese Warship's Misunderstanding: When the water police fired their guns, a Japanese Navy 15th Squadron warship was docked on the nearby river surface. Upon hearing the gunfire, it immediately turned on searchlights to investigate the source of the gunfire. The Japanese warship quickly determined that the gunfire came from the Jiangshun Steamer, so it dispatched a team of soldiers to inspect the steamer.

Wanting to Conduct an Inspection: The Japanese warship immediately dispatched a team of navy soldiers, led by an officer, and launched a small launch, carrying the soldiers to the front of the Nanshi Pier and arbitrarily entering our country's merchant ship. The Jiangshun owner, Mai Dehui'an, came out to stop them. The Japanese soldiers asked where the gunfire came from, and the shipowner explained that the gunfire was from the Chinese water police who were carrying out inspection duties on the ship, so there was gunfire, and it had nothing to do with the Japanese warship. At this time, the water police on board had been persuaded to leave by the shipowner. The Japanese navy initially insisted on conducting an inspection, but after the shipowner repeatedly refused for half an hour, they finally retreated.

Reporting to the Authorities: After the Japanese soldiers retreated, the water police came to the ship twice more and searched out two packages of opium. At that time, because Qian Caiyun's injuries were very serious, the three stokers were taken away. Afterwards, the four injured sailors were sent to a certain hospital by the bureau for treatment. Regarding the people on board who were found with opium, they firmly denied it. Yesterday, the bureau had reported the situation of the water police's inspection of opium, the conflict with the sailors, and the gunfire causing a misunderstanding by the Japanese navy, which sent armed soldiers to the ship and forcibly wanted to search it, to the municipal government, requesting negotiations with the Japanese side to stop it, so as to avoid similar incidents from happening again.

Team Member's Talk: Our reporter made a special visit to the Water Patrol Team yesterday. According to a team member of the team, in the past two months, the team has repeatedly cracked major cases of large quantities of opium on various steamers sailing on the Yangtze River. Because the team is responsible for its duties, it has not dared to neglect in the slightest. Therefore, whenever a steamer arrives at the port, it must be inspected in accordance with the order. Moreover, when the Jiangshun Steamer set sail from Hankou, the team had received a tip that the steamer was carrying a large quantity of opium in its fire room this time. Therefore, when the steamer arrived at the port, the team leader and police officers immediately went on board to search it that night. Unexpectedly, at that time, because there were few of us and many of them, those guys dared to seize guns from the police officers and at the same time used wooden sticks and iron rulers to resist arrest. For the sake of self-defense, the police officers had to fire warning shots, and as a result, one of the police officers of the team was seriously injured, which also shows the barbarity of those guys at that time. But in the end, two sacks of opium, totaling nine large packages, were found in the fire room of the steamer, and three people were arrested by the police and sent to the Judicial Section together. As for the Japanese navy's misunderstanding at that time, the team was not responsible for it. The team leader has reported the situation to the bureau chief and the mayor for verification.

Sichuan Provincial Government Telegram 61

Tibetan Bandits Still Plan to Counterattack

Sichuan-Xikang Army, Knowing Their Deceptive Plan, Rapidly Seizes Chamdo

The Sichuan Provincial Government Office in Shanghai received a telegram from the Sichuan Provincial Government yesterday, saying that it had received a telegram from Kangding stating that after our (Sichuan-Xikang) army captured Dege and other counties, the Tibetan bandits, in order to buffer, were both asking us for peace and actively trying to cross the Jinsha River to counterattack.旅長 Yu Ruhai旅長 has already telegraphed Liu Zongzhihui (Wenhui) to instruct everything and ordered his troops to join forces with the troops from Xining to attack Chamdo quickly. The Tibetan bandits have no base in Kang, and they must withdraw from the country. In recent days, our side has been very victorious. Chamdo can be taken within days. Also, the officers and soldiers of our vanguard troops in the Tibetan expedition who died in the Zhucheng Chase Egg Formation on the 删除th (15th) of the month greatly shook the morale of the front line that day, and they all wanted to win the final victory to lay the foundation for Xikang and consolidate the border.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Advises Various Industries 62

Domestic Goods Should Be Carried by Domestic Ships

Mutual Relationship Is the Only Way to Survive

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to various trade associations and the four major commodity groups yesterday, saying that the letter from the Municipal Shipping Trade Association on the 14th stated that "Chinese people use domestic goods, domestic goods are loaded on domestic ships, and domestic ships use domestic coal. This mutual relationship and mutual obligation must not be interrupted or neglected. Now that domestic ships use domestic coal, the industry has painfully realized this. Chinese people also use domestic goods, which is gradually becoming widespread. However, domestic goods loaded on domestic ships has not been fully implemented. It has been found that most of the various domestic goods in the city that are produced by factories and distributed to other ports are still loaded on foreign ships. The cigarettes of the Nanyang Huacheng Tobacco Company are the most numerous and most famous. Other domestic goods are too numerous to mention. This mutual relationship is therefore interrupted, and this mutual obligation is therefore neglected. To infer its influence and seek its results, it is feared that it is not only our domestic ships that have no hope of survival. Your association is the center of various industries, and it will definitely not discriminate in supervising its members. Now that you have warned domestic ships must use domestic coal, and you have not issued a warning for domestic goods not to be loaded on domestic ships, it must be because the investigation has not been completed and no one has reported it. Our association has seen and heard it, and we dare to send you a letter. We respectfully hope that you will examine it and quickly give a practical warning. From now on, all domestic goods in the city and all factories manufacturing domestic goods that are shipped to other ports must be carried entirely by domestic ships, so as to help each other survive and show their determination to save the country." Our country has been economically invaded by the great powers, and the losses incurred over the years are enormous. Now that the national crisis has not ended, all citizens should be vigilant and self-disciplined and seek ways to save the country. Even a small amount of money used in peacetime should be carefully selected for its destination to identify its advantages and disadvantages. Unless it is absolutely necessary, how can we arbitrarily give profits to foreigners and disregard the economic livelihood of our own people? The contents of the letter are pertinent to the times and must be seriously warned. In addition to sending a separate letter, we hereby write to your association to check and advise your members that from now on, all goods shipped to other ports must be carried by domestic ships in order to promote them and avoid the outflow of rights and interests. This is what we hope for.

Yesterday Afternoon 63

Bombing at Minghua Store

Two Panes of Glass Shattered

Customers Were Greatly Frightened

The Minghua Silk and Satin Store at No. 485 Nanjing Road received a warning from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group on August 20, saying that the store had re-sold the inferior goods that had been sealed up. The store immediately published a statement in the newspaper. Unexpectedly, at around 1:30 PM yesterday afternoon, when customers were crowded, a teenager in a gray long gown suddenly went up to the second floor in a hurry. Before long, he came down and walked to the middle of the store, where he shouted for customers to evacuate quickly. Then he threw a bomb into the store and ran away. But the explosive force was not strong, so no one was injured. Only two panes of glass facing the street were shattered. The Old Gate Police Station was informed and immediately sent detectives to investigate. They also picked up the exploded iron fragments and kept them for the record. It is heard that the store received another warning letter after the incident, explaining the reason for throwing the bomb.

Zhenru Municipal Committee Submits Document to the Mayor 67

Requesting Consultation with the Ministry of Railways to Change Original Land Acquisition Plan

Hong Lanxiang and Wang Shouyu, municipal committee members of the Zhenru District of Shanghai Municipality, submitted a document to the mayor yesterday, stating, "We are submitting this report based on the actual situation. Seven or eight out of ten residents in our district are farmers, and they rely on the income from cultivation for their livelihood. Farmers cannot survive without land to cultivate. The area of our district is less than 50,000 mu. After deducting rivers, roads, markets, villages, residences, and graveyards, there are only 30,000 mu of arable land. The farmers of more than 4,000 households already feel that there is not enough land. In the past ten years, land has been acquired in our district for Jinan School, Jinan New Village in 1924, and International Radio Telegraph in 1929. The area acquired by these three entities is more than 1,000 mu, resulting in the displacement of hundreds of farming households. Now, there is a proposal to relocate the Joint Transportation Terminal of the Ministry of Railways to Zhenru, and the land to be acquired extends west beyond Taopu to Jingtang, east to Wangjiajing Residence, south to Caijia Residence, and north to the Beijing-Shanghai Road, amounting to about 4,000 mu, almost one-tenth of the entire district's area. If this matter is carried out, at least 1,000 households in our district will lose their livelihoods. If these people, who depend on the land for their livelihood, lose the land they rely on for survival, how will they make a living? Living elsewhere is not their strength. If they leave their hometowns and go elsewhere, where in this vast land will they find a place to settle down? While the district committees were at a loss, this morning, hundreds of villagers, including Li Juqing, Li Bo, Zeng Zhi, and Hou Zhuoting, spontaneously gathered, bringing the old and the young, to request that we forward their plea to the mayor to find a way to stop this, so that they can eke out a living. Because this matter concerns the livelihood of farmers, we request that the mayor promptly consult with the Ministry of Railways to change the original plan and find another suitable location, so that the farmers in our district, who have survived the catastrophe, can barely survive. This would be a great act of benevolence. Respectfully submitted to Wu, the Mayor of Shanghai."

Villagers in Enclosed Villages Petition the Railway Bureau 70

The Railway Bureau Indicates That the Base Has Not Yet Been Determined

The Ministry of Railways is building a joint transportation terminal for two railways between Zhenru and Pengpu. The villages of Wangjiajing and Wangjiazai, north of Jiaotong Road, believe that their villages can be avoided. They petitioned the municipal government for relief some time ago. This newspaper reported yesterday that representatives were sent to the Two-Railway Administration to petition. The situation is detailed below:

Petition Situation: Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, village representative Hou Xuanqing petitioned the Two-Railway Administration on Baziluka, where he was received by Secretary Ding Zhenheng. The representative briefly stated that most of the villagers are farmers. Now that the farmland is about to be completely bought up, and the village houses are also enclosed, the villagers' livelihoods will be cut off. The suffering in the future is unimaginable. Although transportation is for the benefit of the country and the people, the problem of people's livelihood should also be taken into account. After investigation, the villages of Wangjiajing and Wangjiazai north of Jiaotong Road can be avoided in terms of geographical situation and railway construction. Therefore, we specifically request Director Chen to forward the request to the Ministry of Railways for relief, and to request that it be submitted to the Two-Railway Rehabilitation Meeting for discussion to allow avoidance, which the villagers will be extremely grateful for. Secretary Ding replied that the Railway Bureau also understands the suffering of the people, so the villages should be avoided as much as possible to alleviate the people's difficulties. The villagers' intention is to ask Director Chen to forward it to the Ministry of Railways for approval.

Railway Bureau's Statement: Yesterday, a Datong News Agency reporter specifically asked Chen Xinghan, Director of the Two-Railway Administration, for his opinion on the matter of the villagers in the villages enclosed by the Ministry of Railways requesting avoidance. Secretary Ding kindly received the reporter on his behalf. He said that the Ministry of Railways, in order to rehabilitate Shanghai and facilitate transportation, will relocate the North Station and build a joint transportation terminal. Director Chen had previously submitted a plan for the rehabilitation of the two railways to the Ministry of Railways. The Ministry of Railways then formed a Two-Railway Rehabilitation Committee to be in charge of the matter. All rehabilitation plans for the two railways are discussed and decided by the committee. Regarding the relocation of the North Station of the two railways and the construction of the joint transportation station, it was previously planned to purchase four to five hundred mu of private land. Officials sent by the Ministry of Railways have been carrying out surveying work in recent days, which has not yet been completed. The land enclosed has not yet been determined. However, the area surveyed is very large, which is to prevent speculators from taking the opportunity to buy and sell. Therefore, the current enclosure is temporary in nature. In the future, a location must be selected within the current enclosure. Whether there are villages in the current enclosure that can be avoided is a matter handled by the Ministry of Railways and the Public Works Bureau. I am not very clear about it. However, it is a fact that the villagers are suffering after the village is enclosed. I think the Ministry of Railways will decide to allow avoidance within the possible range.

Public Concession 73

Labor Dispute at the Tram Company

Union Executive Dismissed by the Company

Social Affairs Bureau Has Sent Personnel to Investigate

All workers in the Vehicle and Machine Departments of the Public Concession Tram Company prepared to organize the Third District Hydroelectric Industry Union last year. On January 1st of this year, under the guidance of Party and government agencies, it was formally established. Unexpectedly, Executive Directors He Zhaoming and others were dismissed by the company, which caused a labor strike. The Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to investigate yesterday in order to conduct mediation.

Union Submission: The Third District Hydroelectric Industry Union submitted a document to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, stating, "Submission for Forwarding. According to the union case, Executive Director He Zhaoming and others reported, 'Submission for Request. I, Zhaoming, have been working as a coppersmith in the British Tram Company for many years. Unfortunately, since September 1931, I have been ill and requested leave according to regulations, which was approved. As the illness has not yet healed, I have requested and been granted an extension of leave. Due to the illness, the delay lasted until January 4th of this year, when I recovered slightly and went to the company to cancel my leave and resume work. Unexpectedly, the company supervisor (British) ordered that Zhaoming and others be suspended from their duties and not be allowed to resume work. I replied on the basis of reason that I had not violated the regulations and there were no acts of negligence. I still requested to be allowed to resume work in order to ensure my livelihood. Not only did the supervisor not grant my request, but he also said that he had learned that I was active outside organizing a union, and therefore dismissed me. According to law, workers are allowed to organize unions, and this does not hinder my duties. How can the company dismiss me on this pretext? I immediately reported to your union and requested that it be forwarded for negotiation. Later, due to the rampant violence of the January 28th Incident, union affairs were suspended, and the matter was delayed. Now it has been restored to its original state. I have to ask your union to forward it to the Party and government agencies to send personnel to negotiate with the company to allow me to resume work, and to demand that the unpaid wages be paid in full. This is a matter of public convenience.' According to this, the employee has been working in the British Tram Company for many years and has never had any negligence. Since November of last year, he has enthusiastically initiated the organization of a union and legally submitted an application. He was elected as a preparatory committee member. He had been responsible for all union affairs. During his responsible period, he became ill and applied for leave from the company. Since the preparatory work was completed and was being established, and the illness was also cured, he went to the company to resume work. Unexpectedly, the company dismissed him for organizing the union, and he has been unemployed for more than eight months. The livelihood of his family is difficult to describe. The union believes that the employee lost his job due to public affairs, and the company unreasonably dismissed the worker, resulting in no effective guarantee for workers' work. The situation is very pitiful. Therefore, we have submitted this document to request that your union bureau investigate and send personnel to negotiate with the company for reinstatement and to demand that the wages during the suspension period be paid in full in order to facilitate union activities and ensure security. Respectfully submitted."

Authorities Investigate: After the establishment of the Third District Hydroelectric Union, the Tram Company dismissed Executive Director He Zhaoming (machine worker), Gong Hongfa (machine worker), and Fang Xiuyan (vehicle worker) on the pretext of dismissal. All the workers heard about it and believed that the company was undermining union activities, and they were very angry. It is reported that the Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhu Guilin, a mediator from the Third Section, to investigate yesterday in order to conduct mediation.

Since the Zhabei Charity Association opened the second congee kitchen on Liuying Road last month, it has been nearly two months. Local News Two

Wicked Son Attacks with Wine Bottle 76

Father Bleeds Profusely

Father and Son Become Enemies Over Sale of Ancestral Property

Family Feud Erupts at Mid-Autumn Festival Feast

Father and Son Each Have a Witness

Two Witnesses Are Also Father and Son

Lu Gentao, a local resident, is currently fifty years old and works as a Hongbang tailor. His son, Lu Jinbao, is twenty-six years old and works as a coppersmith in the machine shop of a certain factory. Since childhood, he has been adopted by Lu Zhao, a woman of the same clan, as her adopted son. Last autumn, Lu Gentao sold a piece of ancestral land to his nephew Lu Changming (the eldest son of Lu Jinbao's brother Lu Jintao). After receiving the money, Lu Jinbao came forward to claim that he wanted to share in the proceeds. Gentao refused to give him any money since Jinbao had already been adopted out and had no right to inherit, and a grudge between the father and son grew. One day, Jinbao carried a copper-handled dagger, intending to harm his biological father. His uncle Lu Jintao found out about this and took the knife away, and the matter subsided. Recently, Lu Zhao also wanted to sell the property to Lu Changming, but a dispute arose in the middle, resulting in litigation. Lu Changming sued Zhao in the civil court of the First Special District Court, and Zhao lost the case. The day before yesterday was the lunar Mid-Autumn Festival. Lu Changfa, the second son of Lu Jintao, hosted a lunch for his family at his residence at 3101 Dongyouheng Road. Lu Gentao and his son were both invited. Unexpectedly, just as the relatives and friends were seated and about to eat, Gentao and his son had another conflict over the issue, and Lu Jinbao picked up a wine bottle on the table and hit his father hard on the head, causing a serious injury. Blood flowed all over his face and the glass shattered. Someone reported the incident to the Jiaxing Road Police Station, and Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to arrest Lu Jinbao and take him, along with the broken pieces, to the police station for detention. Lu Gentao was sent to the hospital for treatment. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the summary court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated the above situation, saying, "Please pay attention to Article 298 of the Criminal Law, which states that those who injure their direct ascendants should have their original sentence increased by two-tenths. Therefore, please severely punish him as a warning to those who defy morality." Lu Gentao and his witness Lu Jintao also reported the case, proving that yesterday was the Mid-Autumn Festival, and when they were having lunch, Jintao persuaded the defendant, a young man, not to drink too much, but the defendant did not listen to the good advice and took offense. He picked up the wine bottle on the table and hit Gentao on the head, and then punched him three times, causing injury and bleeding. They also hired attorney Xi Yafu to appear in court and bring a private prosecution, requesting that in addition to the heavy punishment, he be ordered to pay medical expenses of eighty yuan. When questioned, the defendant denied the accusations, saying that the plaintiff had designed to frame him, and that his finger had been bitten by the plaintiff. He also hired attorney Gan Lin to appear in court to defend him. Finally, the defendant invited his witness Lu Changfa (Lu Jintao's second son) to testify, saying, "Yesterday was the Mid-Autumn Festival, and I invited the clansmen to lunch. The plaintiff suddenly came and dragged the defendant out and beat him in the courtyard. I did not see the defendant hit the plaintiff with a wine bottle." Lu Jintao and his son acted as witnesses for the plaintiff and the defendant, respectively, which was a funny thing. Then the lawyers from both sides began to debate, and Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the case and announced that the debate in the case was over and the sentence would be pronounced next Monday. The defendant was remanded in custody. It is unknown how this case of moral outrage will end.

Yesterday's High Tide in This Port 77

Maximum Height Reached Over Thirty-Nine Feet

In past autumn floods, the tide would rise violently, damaging crops, causing great concern to farmers. However, since the autumn floods this year, the tide has not been very high, so the rice crops in the four villages of Songjiang have not been damaged. This flood was the largest of the year. Since the day before yesterday (15th), the tide has been high. The maximum daily tide has risen to thirty-eight feet (customs water scale), and the evening tide has risen to more than thirty-eight feet. Yesterday, due to the northeast wind, the tide rose even higher, and the water was red, with rapid currents rising to more than thirty-nine feet. The tide in the Wusong Yunzaobang was level with the outer road. If it rises another half a foot, it will rush into the road, and residents may suffer again. Fortunately, although it is a northeast wind, the east is large and the north is small. If the north is large and the east is small, the residents would be unimaginable.

Ruling on the Three Friends Dispute 78

Officials Urge Company to Comply

Company Appeals the Ruling

Workers Resume Hunger Strike This Morning

Yesterday, Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, sent a telegram to Mayor Wu of Shanghai regarding the labor dispute and closure of the Yinxiang Port factory of the Sanyou Industrial Society, urging the company to comply with the arbitration award. The company defied the order and refused to pay for meals. The municipal government and other parties met yesterday to discuss solutions. Details are as follows:

Company Has Appealed: Following the ruling by the Shanghai Labor-Management Arbitration Committee on August 31 regarding the labor dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Society, the company immediately expressed its disagreement. Several days ago, it prepared a petition and dispatched Managing Directors Shen Jiucheng and Wang Xianhua, Acting Factory Manager Lao Huimin, and Secretary Chief Ji Jiannan to the local court to file an appeal. Regarding the meal expenses of more than 1,200 workers in the factory, amounting to 120 yuan per day, the company, citing financial burden, refused to pay.

Chairman Chiang’s Telegram: Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, sent a telegram to Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai, which stated in brief, "The arbitration decision on the labor dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Society Cotton Mill is appropriate. It is hoped that the company will be persuaded to comply with the arbitration award."

Municipal Government Order: The Municipal Government issued an order to the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating, "For compliance with the order, according to a petition submitted by Zhang Yihai and others, standing directors of the 7th District Cotton Textile Industry Union, the company is deliberately appealing and suspending the payment of meal expenses. It is requested that emergency measures be taken to value human life." Based on this, a copy of the petition is attached, ordering the bureau to promptly instruct the company to continue to maintain meal expenses until the case is resolved. This order is issued.

Suspension of Meal Expenses: Yesterday afternoon around 2:00 PM, six representatives from the 7th District Cotton Textile Industry Union, including Xia Zhongzhao, Qin Changgeng, Bao Boyi, Zhang Tingliang, Wu Renfu, and Qin Haiyan, went to the Social Affairs Bureau to collect meal expenses for two periods. The company still refused to pay. Representative Wang Xianqing from the Social Affairs Bureau then went to the Municipal Government to discuss effective solutions to quickly resolve the meal expenses issue, in order to prevent accidents.

Workers Still on Hunger Strike: After hearing the news, the workers residing at the Labor Hospital immediately stated that if the meal expenses could not be received, they would continue the hunger strike. Because the company still did not provide meals yesterday, the workers continued their hunger strike this morning. The list of names is as follows: Hong Jiaben, Liu Yushan, Sun Xuren, Lu Shiying, Gong Yushu, Yin Mingzhang, Xie Yonggui, Zhang Zegang, Yan Qilang, Li Yinsheng, Mao Zhaocheng, Shen Yucheng, Fan Yinchuan, Hou Zhangyuan, Ma Jinchun, Zhao Weiyin, Liu Yuanxing, Gao Jinshan.

The Qiuxin Factory Labor Unrest Was Heard Yesterday 79

Party and Government Mediation Still Yields No Results

The Company Proposes Three Demands

According to the Dagong News Agency, after a strike broke out at the Shanghai Army Camp Qiuxin Shipyard, the Party and government repeatedly sent representatives to mediate. Because the company's attitude was tough, there was no hope for a solution at the time. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Dai Yongchan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Zhu Jintao, representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, went to the Qiuxin Factory in the Shanghai Army Camp for negotiations. Mr. Medilo received them and stated that he was unable to handle the case at the moment, so he had telegraphed the general company in France to inquire about solutions. Finally, he added that the Party and government representatives could consult with the executives of the Shanghai General Company in Yangjingbang, which might lead to a reasonable solution. Therefore, the Party and government representatives went to the General Company again in the afternoon for negotiations. The general manager of the company received them and explained the intention of the Party and government agencies to mediate, and proposed two solutions: (1) The dismissed workers should return to work; (2) Wages should be paid as usual for the strike period. At that time, the general manager of the company agreed and requested two points from the Party and government agencies: (1) Be responsible for ensuring that all workers return to work; (2) Guarantee that similar incidents will not happen again in the future. The Party and government representatives replied that the first point was fully accepted, and that there would be no problem with the second point if the company did not oppress the workers. While the two sides were negotiating, Mr. Mai, the manager of Qiuxin Factory, unexpectedly intervened, insisting on dismissing the workers, and said that if the workers were allowed to return to work, the factory's face would be completely lost. After listening to Mr. Mai's words, the company's general manager completely overturned the previous agreement and proposed three unreasonable principles for resuming work: (1) Workers must return to work unconditionally by the 18th; (2) Salaries will be acknowledged one-third up to the 16th; (3) Worker No. 821 must be dismissed. At that time, the Party and government representatives refuted this, saying that the fault for the current labor unrest lies with the company, and that unreasonable conditions should not be proposed again. Thus, the two sides went to extremes, and at 4:00 PM, they dispersed without any results.

Yangtze River Shipping Fees Changed to Cash 80

Starting September 16th

China Merchants, Jardine Matheson, Sanbei, Taikoo, Hongan, Jiejjiang, Zhaoxing, Ningshao, Minsheng, Jufu and other ten companies issued a notice yesterday, which reads: To whom it may concern, our companies transport goods exported from Shanghai to the upper, middle, and lower reaches of the Yangtze River and various ports in Hunan. The shipping fees are mostly paid monthly or seasonally. In recent years, the cost of various commodities has been high and expenses have increased daily. Moreover, all expenditures require cash, making turnover quite difficult. After public discussion, starting from September 16th, all shipping fees for goods shipped to the above-mentioned routes will be collected in cash or bank drafts (for a maximum of ten days). If the shipping fees are not paid in Shanghai, then the shipped goods must pay the shipping fees in full upon arrival at their destination before they can be picked up. Please forgive all customs brokers and import-export firms. This notice is hereby given.

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Prevents 81

Foreign Merchants from Installing Telephones Beyond Borders

The Telephone Company Should Bear Full Responsibility for Delaying the Contract

Since the expiration of the telephone contract between the former China-Foreign German Telephone Company and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, the American-owned Shanghai Telephone Company's installation of telephones beyond its borders in the urban area has been stopped by the Bureau of Public Utilities. On the one hand, the bureau urged the company and the Telephone Bureau to negotiate a temporary contract for transition. Unexpectedly, although the company had signed and approved the draft agreement in October of last year, it has delayed signing the formal contract until now. Citizens, unaware of the details of the case, still apply to the telephone company for telephone installation. However, the company does not explain the reasons why installation is not possible, but instead instructs them to request a special permit from the Bureau of Public Utilities, hoping to shift responsibility. It was learned yesterday that the Bureau of Public Utilities specifically issued a letter stating that the company should bear responsibility for delaying the contract and should subsequently explain to users that it has not yet obtained exclusive operating rights and directly refuse installations, in order to dispel public misunderstandings. The original letter is excerpted below: Greetings, regarding the case of your company operating a telephone business in the road sections beyond the boundaries of the public concession and the French concession, since the Bureau, together with the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and your company, respectively stamped and signed the draft temporary contract in October of last year, your company has delayed until now and has not indicated when the formal contract will be signed. This is regrettable. Before the temporary contract is formally established, your company should not install telephones in the above-mentioned sections according to law. Recently, it has been found that users residing in the sections have requested your company to install telephones, but your company does not immediately explain the reasons why installation is not possible and directly refuses it. Instead, it instructs them to request a special permit from the Bureau. This move on your company's part is nothing more than an attempt to delegate to the Bureau the responsibility for causing inconvenience to citizens. However, after the Bureau explained the details of the negotiation of the temporary contract in detail, most users were able to understand. In order to avoid unnecessary trouble for citizens, your company should, in the future, immediately explain that it has not yet obtained exclusive operating rights for telephones in these sections when encountering requests to install telephones in these sections, and refuse installation directly. Do not make excuses or shirk responsibility. Sincerely, to the Shanghai Telephone Company.

Public Groups in Various Provinces and Cities 82

Respond to the Case of the Invasion of Asia-Europe and Are Willing to Vow Support

Regarding the case of the products of the Chinese Asia-Europe Electric Appliance Factory being excluded from sales in Southeast Asia by the Philips light bulb company, the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products and the China National Products Maintenance Association, in order to protect the interests of members and safeguard overseas trade, advocate serious negotiations. In addition to sending telegrams to various agencies to protest, they also sent letters to relevant public groups in various provinces and cities requesting assistance. According to telegrams from electrical industry trade associations and national products organizations in Hankou, Shantou, Tianjin, Qingdao, Chengdu, Beiping, Nanchang, Tangzhou, Kaifeng, Shanghai, the capital (Nanjing), Jinan, Hangzhou, Taiyuan, Fuzhou, Xiamen, Wuhu, Bengbu, Zhenjiang, Zhengzhou and other places, they successively replied, expressing unanimous support and vowing to be a backing force. Excerpts from the original letters are as follows: (1) Quick telegram from Hankou Electrical Materials Industry Trade Association, (omitted above) "Approved the telegram from your association that the electric bulbs produced by the Chinese Asia-Europe Electric Appliance Factory are sold in Java. Because of the suitability of quality and price, they are envied by the Dutch Philips Company, which makes slanderous accusations and excludes them in every possible way. Finally, the local authorities ordered them to stop selling, and they are still not satisfied, and even further demanded compensation for losses. How can this not cause grief and indignation! Since the opening of ports and seas, all countries have treaties for trade and protect each other without discrimination. However, the actions of the Dutch merchants are outside the scope of free commercial competition, and their authorities are also shielding them and striking overseas trade in violation of the spirit of the treaty. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? Our merchants, in order to respect the development of national rights and interests, and not to implement the purpose of commercial treaty reciprocity, the real economy will be lost, and there is no hope for the future. Your association's duty lies in taking responsibility. I hope you will do your best to support so that negotiations can be resolved fairly and there is no disturbance in overseas trade. Otherwise, we will treat them in the same way, using profits to resist them. Our association is closely related and vows to be a backing force." (Omitted below) (2) Telegram from Chao-Mei National Products Industry and Commerce Federation, (omitted above) "Since foreign insults have become increasingly urgent and the national situation has become weaker, the initial rise of national products is like a baby leaving the wall to learn to walk, and there is always a fear of falling. What is relied upon is the government and the people, working together to promote and maintain it, like a nanny hoping to grow into an adult easily. Receiving your letter now, I am deeply saddened to learn that the various national electric bulbs produced by the Shanghai Chinese merchant Asia-Europe Electric Appliance Factory have been promoted and sold in the Dutch-occupied territories by the overseas Chinese Qingnian Trading Company. Overseas Chinese have always been angry at the imperialists for their oppressive power and love the applicability of national products, so they do their best to purchase and sell them. Therefore, they have touched the jealousy of the Dutch merchant Philips. Not hesitating to cause international resentment for commercial issues, they instigated the Dutch authorities to destroy them under the pretext that our national product Asia-Europe light bulbs have taken their argon gas and other manufacturing rights. They suddenly oppressed and stopped business with unreasonable problems. Hearing this, I am filled with anger. Hu Xiyuan of Asia-Europe Electric Appliance Factory has worked hard to improve and maintain, so that he has the current situation. Now, the Dutch merchant Philips, in order to protect his own interests, is actually destroying our country's inherent industry. Moreover, the manufacture of commercial goods, except for the new products that can truly be invented independently and obtained the permission of the government in the place of manufacture to issue a license and announce a patent, which can enjoy the exclusive manufacturing rights for several years, what is the so-called encroachment? The Dutch merchant Philips has not obtained the patent announcement from our government, so naturally, it cannot have any effect. What is the crime of counterfeiting? Then, if foreign merchants manufacture various kinds of goods to cater to the habits of our people and sell them in our country's market, can our merchants also say that they are encroaching on exclusive manufacturing rights? In summary, it is extremely unreasonable to make trouble. At this time, our country's national products are declining, and the market is almost completely invaded by foreign goods. Industrial and commercial organizations have repeatedly appealed and petitioned the government. They are trying their best to promote it above, and the people are realizing that the imperialists use cunning and hideous faces as tools for deception and are using national products below. Our association is responsible for protecting national products, and the chairman cannot refuse. I dare to inform the people of the country, to pay attention to promoting national products. The external pressure of the Asia-Europe electric bulbs is not enough to be afraid of. The meeting has already appealed to the Ministry of Industry of the National Government to transfer and consult the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to refute the shamelessness of the Dutch merchants according to reason, and should wait for the instructions and resolve them properly. If the Dutch merchant Philips still does not repent and considers our people to be deceivable, then our association will lead our members and request all compatriots across the country to unanimously not buy the electric bulbs of the Dutch merchant Philips as a way to deal with it. The Chu bow is obtained by the Chu people, and they can dispose of it freely. (Omitted below)

The Social Affairs Bureau Convened Various Industries 83

To Explain the Significance of Factory Inspection

Can Take Care of Factual Issues

The Results of Various Industries Expressing Their Opinions Were Satisfactory

After the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau was ordered to start implementing the initial factory inspection on September 1, various industrial and commercial groups requested a postponement due to the decline of industry and commerce after the war. The bureau specifically convened various groups on the 14th and 15th to explain in detail, and the results were satisfactory. Details are as follows:

Industry Representatives: On the 14th, Li Ruzhang and Yang Zhenxin from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Zhenzhang, Ye Zhangcheng, and Qi Fuming from the Shanghai National Products Factory Federation, and Zhang Zemin from the Chinese Cotton Mill Federation attended. On the 15th, Wan Xuefang from the National Products Rubber Products Industry Association, Xian Guansheng from the Biscuit Candy and Canned Food Industry, Dong Xiyan from the Enamel Industry Association, Cao Runshen from the Lighter and Flower Rolling Industry Association, Zhu Xiaoyun from the Printing Iron Can Industry Association, Xiao Ziming from the Chinese Soap Industry Association, Wang Shiqiang and Jin Yinwu from the Electric Silk Weaving Industry Association, Yang Boru from the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association, Ding Chong from the Refining Industry Association, Hong Weiguan from the Chinese Cigarette Factory Industry Association, Xu Guanqun from the Cosmetics Industry Association, Wang Yaochen from the Flour Mill Industry Association, Fei Xiangxue from the Knitting Industry Association, and Shen Huachen from the Silk Factory Industry Association attended.

Chairman's Explanation: Tian Heqing, Director of the Social Observation Division of the Social Affairs Bureau, who chaired the meeting, elaborated in detail on the meaning of the Factory Law and the Factory Inspection Law promulgated by the state, and informed that it has been a year since the implementation of the two regulations, and the situation of each factory is complex, and compliance is not without difficulty. Therefore, this bureau has carefully considered the scope and method of the initial inspection. The purpose is to gradually eliminate the difficulties of each factory. Factory inspection, on the one hand, is to remind the factory of its legal obligations, and on the other hand, it can provide more opportunities to contact each factory, so that a more accurate view of the actual situation of each industry can be obtained, and all facilities can naturally adapt to the current situation. Then, the matters within the scope of the initial inspection were explained one by one to clarify that each factory does not have any reason to have difficulties. He also said that when factory inspectors carry out inspections, they should consider the actual situation and the difficulties of the factory, and asked them to submit them to the inspectors as much as possible. Finally, the representatives expressed many opinions, some on the general situation of the Factory Law, and some on the special circumstances of each industry. All were explained in detail by the chairman, and the results were very satisfactory.

The Murder Case on Paul Street Concluded 87

The Police Do Not Prosecute the Communists

Sentencing Scheduled for the Morning of the 23rd

Chen Yun (also known as Keming), a Shaoxing native residing at No. 7 Chengxinfang, Paul Street, allegedly used a kitchen knife to injure and kill Wang Zixi (also known as Huang Zixi, 23 years old), a native of Pudong, in the pavilion of the house at around 5:00 AM on the 7th of this month. After the case was discovered, he was arrested and escorted to the First Special District Court by Chinese and Western detectives from the Huishan Police Station. He has repeatedly confessed and details have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Shen Bingrong continued the hearing in the Fourth Criminal Court. Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the police, stated that the communist books seized in the defendant's bedroom in the pavilion of the house were being changed, and the defendant had consistently denied that they were his in the police station, so he would not be prosecuted. Huang Jintang, the father of the deceased, hired a lawyer to file a private suit, stating that the cause of the case was that the defendant had previously borrowed 80 yuan from the deceased and collected 11 yuan in rent privately. He asked him for it that day, which led to the incident. There was no ambiguity with his wife. The private suit now seeks to compensate the defendant for the loan and funeral expenses, totaling 591 yuan. When questioned, Chen Yun confessed that the communist books seized were not his, and there was no such thing as the loan mentioned above. He said that the deceased Huang Zixi came to his place to play and chat that day, and every time he mentioned asking his wife to come to Shanghai to live with him, it touched the hatred in his heart. In addition, he drank too much alcohol at the time and his nerves were disordered, which led to the incident. The court ordered the debate to begin, and the police lawyer Zhang said that the police accused the defendant of premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law, and the deceased suffered a total of 21 knife wounds on the chest, forehead, temples, ears, hands, and other parts, which was tantamount to dismemberment and was extremely cruel. He requested that the defendant be severely punished. Chen Yun was defended by a designated lawyer, Huang Xiubo. Chen finally claimed that he had an elderly mother, wife, and children at home and requested leniency. He had nothing else to say. Judge Shen ordered him to be taken into custody and await sentencing on the morning of the 23rd of this month.

Sentence in the Cao Akun Assassination Case 88

Xu Changyu Sentenced to Thirteen Years in Prison

Cao Akun, a native of Jiangyin residing at No. 50 Renji Road, Pudong, 28 years old, was shot and killed by his enemies at around 4:00 AM on June 28 of this year while playing mahjong in the Ruiji Shenzhuang General Assembly on the third floor of No. 78 Minguo Road in the French Concession. On the same day, Jin Jiulin, supervisor of the special agency of the French police, chief detective Li Yaolong, Zhang Ziying, and detectives on duty arrested Xu Changyu and suspect Wen Baoqiang in Pudong, and sent them to the Second Special Court to file a public prosecution. After repeated hearings by Judge Li Changnian, the defendant Xu Changyu hired lawyer Lan Ren for defense, and Zhou was defended by lawyer Zhu Dianqing. The final debate has been announced, and sentencing is scheduled. Yesterday was the day of sentencing. At 10:00 AM, Judge Li presided over the First Criminal Court and announced the verdict. Xu Changyu was sentenced to thirteen years of imprisonment for the crime of jointly premeditating murder. The number of days of custody before the judgment is final shall be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Zhou Baoqiang was found not guilty.

Fire at Dahuali, Belle Road 89

Wires Exploded and Caused a Fire

Spreading to Four Neighbors

The wire on the third floor of the house of He Yixiang at No. 14 Dahuali, Belle Road, French Concession, suddenly exploded at 8:00 PM last night, causing a fire. The momentum was so fierce that it immediately broke through the roof and spread to Tiansheng Cloth Factory at No. 13 and a certain family at No. 15. Black smoke filled the air and the firelight soared. The residents in the house barely escaped with their lives. Upon receiving the news, the French Concession Fire Brigade immediately drove to the scene to put out the fire and tried to cut off the wires to prevent the fire from spreading. However, the fire was raging and difficult to extinguish for a while. As a result, the Yang family at No. 16 was also burned, and the fire spread to No. 17. After the firefighters bravely put out the fire until around 9:30 PM, the momentum was slightly reduced. An investigation after the incident showed that all houses from No. 13 to No. 16 were completely burned, and the three-story building at No. 17 was also burned. Among them, only Tiansheng Cloth Factory had fire insurance of 18,000 taels.

Liu Guixin Died After Drunk Fall from a Vehicle 90

A Tragic Accident of Being Crushed to Death

Liu Guixin, the owner of Santaiyuan, Guizhi Road, Wusong, 31 years old, was honest and trustworthy and had made outstanding achievements in handling local public welfare and fire prevention matters on weekdays. He went to Shanghai a few days ago for business and drank with friends. Later, he returned to Song by train at 5:25 PM. It is said that Liu was drunk and slightly abnormal. When the train arrived at Yunzaobang Station, before it had stopped, he jumped down, lost his balance, and fell under the platform, crushing his waist. At that time, he hired a car to send him to Shanghai Baolong Hospital for treatment, but the injury was internal and could not be recovered. He returned to his Wusong residence by car the day before yesterday and died in Song around 8:00 PM in the evening. People in Song who heard the news lamented.

Children Should Not Play on the Road 91

Liu Hongkui Was Tragically Run Over and Killed by a Car

Liu Hongkui, the nine-year-old only son of Liu Binggen, a Wuxi native who works in the printing industry and resides at No. 2 Sanxinli, Ellegrant Road, French Concession, was running and playing with his companions and neighbor children on the road in front of the Dingjili gate on the west side of the Empire Cinema on Avenue Joffre at 11:00 PM on the 9th of this month. At that time, a business car driven by car driver Zhang Wenhe from Yitai Motor Company was driving from west to east. The Liu child did not have time to dodge and was knocked down, injuring his head, lower abdomen, feet, and other parts. The patrolman arrived, copied the number, and sent the injured person and car to Renji Hospital for treatment. He also returned to the police station to report to the head detective for verification. Liu child died in the hospital at 3:10 PM on the afternoon of the day before yesterday due to serious injuries that could not be treated. The hospital notified the police station to send the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall morgue. Yesterday morning, the vehicle management office reported to the Second Special Court and appointed Prosecutor Deng Baosun to visit the morgue with the coroner to examine the body. Deng Jun then stated that it was found that Liu Hongkui had been injured and killed by a car, and the body was buried by the family after signing a guarantee.

Ordinary teams such as Shi Mengjiu with 400 points, Wei Bozheng with 250 points, Qi Wuyi with 250 points, Zhang Hanchang with 220 points, Shen Cihu with 222 points, Chuan Daiyun with 220 points, and Zhu Jiuru with 211 points also exceeded the quota. It is also said that the total number of points collected is approximately 20,000.

Exclusive Logo for Chinese-Owned Manufacturers

The Silk and Satin Printing Industry Association of this city, noting that non-Chinese printing factories have recently become very active and that some despicable peddlers are acting as their running dogs, falsely claiming to represent various factories and brands to solicit silk orders from silk shops, making it difficult for the shops to distinguish between genuine and fake, has specially prepared silver circular badges and peddler permits with the user's photo for the peddlers of each member factory to wear, in order to provide easy identification for customers. If customers have any doubts, they can ask to see the badge and permit to avoid deception. It is reported that the badges and permits are already in use and have been announced in the newspaper.

Letter to the Editor

The True Meaning of Responsible Freight Transportation 110

Yu Yan, Director of the Railway Business Department

Speech at the Central Broadcasting Station

The topic I will discuss today is "The Significance of Responsible Freight Transportation and Its Relationship to National Economy and People's Livelihood." What is responsible freight transportation? Simply put, responsible freight transportation means that the railway assumes considerable responsibility for the goods entrusted by the shippers, from the moment the goods are received until they are transported to the destination and delivered to the consignee. Within this timeframe, the railway must assume corresponding custody responsibilities, the responsibility for safe and prompt transportation, and the corresponding responsibility for compensation for damages. In other words, the railway treats the shippers' goods as if they were its own, striving to ensure that they are not subject to any damage or delay and are delivered intact to the consignee. Unless due to force majeure events such as natural disasters, or changes in the nature of the goods themselves, or the shipper's own negligence, if the goods are lost, the railway is liable for compensation.

Railways in all countries around the world are responsible for the goods entrusted by shippers. They do their best to provide convenience and happiness to merchants. All damages to goods that should not have occurred under the railway's responsibility are compensated. Since the responsibility borne by the railway is very heavy, its equipment and personnel must strive for thoroughness and perfection. Shippers also have increasing trust in the railway. In name, the railway and merchants are separate, but in fact, they are one. Therefore, their railway freight increases day by day, and the business of the general public develops day by day. National strength is naturally a major reason. However, looking back at the situation of our Chinese railways regarding freight, our railways have never assumed any responsibility for the goods they transport. Because they are not responsible, the railway's equipment is as good as it can be, and the railway staff are as perfunctory as they can be. Over time, employees have developed bureaucratic bad habits, and the railway has lost its original business essence. Goods entrusted to the railway for transportation not only have no security guarantee, but also experience various inconveniences. Shippers, due to capital constraints, have to find other ways out. Therefore, various malpractices have arisen. The most obvious is the forwarding company. In order to avoid the trouble of dealing with bureaucratic railway employees and to ensure the safety of their goods and avoid losses, shippers have to entrust forwarding companies to report and transport goods to the railway on their behalf. Forwarding companies, driven by profits, seize the opportunity to monopolize and arbitrarily manipulate prices, or even collude with unscrupulous station employees, manipulating things from top to bottom. General shippers are greatly exploited. For more than fifty years, railway freight has declined day by day, and the suffering of merchants has increased day by day. It has reached the point where shippers can hardly survive, and the railway is gradually approaching bankruptcy. If we do not have any fundamental solutions, we can only wait for everyone to perish together.

This dangerous situation was seen as early as ten years ago, and the Chinese people have long wanted to find ways to remedy it. Therefore, at the National Railway Transportation Conference convened by the former Ministry of Communications in the tenth year of the Republic, it was decided to implement responsible freight transportation, and the general rules for responsible transportation were promulgated at the same time. However, due to various reasons, the various routes did not thoroughly and conscientiously implement it. These ten years have passed in vain. The various malpractices of railway freight are deeper than before, and the suffering of merchants is greater than before. Now, no matter which aspect you consider, freight on various routes can no longer be fundamentally rectified. The only way to rectify freight is to implement responsible transportation. Because the implementation of responsible transportation increases the railway's responsibility to shippers, equipment will naturally be required to be improved, and employees will naturally have to work diligently and not allow any perfunctoriness. Merchants transporting goods can follow a regular path and obtain real convenience. All past accumulated malpractices can be fundamentally eradicated. Only by fundamentally eradicating all kinds of accumulated malpractices can we talk about developing commerce, developing the social economy, and seeking happiness for the general public. This is the biggest motivation and the most important purpose of the Ministry of Railways' resolute implementation of responsible transportation this time.

Responsible freight transportation is a fundamental principle of railway freight transportation. Violating this principle means that the railway is abandoning its mission, and naturally there will be no good results. The reason why our railways have the current poor state and merchants feel extreme pain is because of violating this principle. After we implement responsible transportation, we can not only reverse the previous poor results, but also have unlimited hope for the future. This is a natural principle and can be asserted. Take the Jinpu and Jinghu routes, which started implementing responsible transportation on September 1st. The staff of all stations implementing responsible transportation have completely changed their past practices due to responsibility, and their work spirit has also been completely commercialized. Shippers also feel various benefits. Shippers who had doubts and misunderstandings about responsible transportation have gradually understood. Therefore, the responsible freight of the two routes is increasing day by day. On the first day of opening on September 1st, the responsible freight on the Jinpu route was 340 tons, and on the Jinghu Huhangyong route, it was 140 tons. In the ten days since then, the Jinpu route has increased to 2,510 tons, and the Jinghu Huhangyong route has increased to 2,580 tons. Generally, shippers have sent letters requesting the two routes to actively expand the responsible measures, praising them. This shows the urgent need for responsible transportation for general shippers. From this, we can imagine what the result will be if the entire station of the two routes is fully implemented, and then imagine what the result will be if all routes across the country are fully implemented. We can resolutely say that after all routes are uniformly implementing responsible transportation in the future, responsible combined transportation, water and land combined transportation, and international combined transportation can be organized. At that time, the national industry and commerce will inevitably develop day by day, and the social economy will inevitably become more and more developed. Only then will the railway truly fulfill its mission.

A small number of merchants and a small number of forwarding companies inevitably have suspicions about responsible transportation due to special relationships. This is really because they have not clearly understood the true face and spirit of responsible transportation, and they have not taken a long-term view. We need to think thoroughly about how our industry and commerce have reached this point of decline, and how the people's livelihood has reached this dangerous period. We have no other way to save it but to seek a way out from reform and construction. We should not forget the long-term interests of the future because of past habits or current interests. Responsible transportation is to seek permanent solutions for general shippers, and to seek permanent solutions for the national economy and people's livelihood, not just to seek benefits for the railway itself. If the social and economic problems are solved, all industries across the country will naturally benefit. If we only care about our own current small profits, what is the use of asking whether the forwarding industry can survive independently until the railway goes bankrupt and the various industries go bankrupt? If we understand this principle, we naturally don't have to doubt it. Moreover, after the implementation of responsible transportation, the smooth flow of freight transportation and the business of transportation companies will naturally develop day by day, so there is no need to worry too much.

In a word, responsible transportation is the only way to rectify the railway transportation in our country, and it is also the fundamental way to relieve the suffering of the merchants and develop the social economy. All sectors of the country must unite and cooperate to complete this major event. This is the ardent hope of the Ministry, and it is also the ardent hope of the national public.

Essay

From China's Current Education to the Establishment of Public Libraries 112

— Wen Bing

Historically, education in China, both past and present, has been almost entirely monopolized by the wealthy class. Before the Qing Dynasty, if you were not from a family with deep roots and ample financial resources, you could not hope to study well, let alone pass the imperial examinations. Because that kind of antiquated education required you to read the Four Books and Five Classics from the very beginning, no matter how hard you worked, the first two or three years were always wasted. At most, you could only recognize a few words, and it was very difficult to apply them to life. Therefore, the poor had no fortune and could only remain ignorant generation after generation. Later, influenced by Western civilization, the system was hastily abolished during the Guangxu reign and replaced with school education. The original intention was to popularize education, but the reality was quite different. Because politics were not on track, ambitious politicians seized power and used educational institutions as places to cultivate their personal influence and recruit party members. Therefore, the sacred field of education often turned into a base and vile drama, and a distorted phenomenon formed, namely, everyone flocked to the development of higher education and universities, neglecting the basic lower-level education. Therefore, the longer schools were run, the less education was popularized. In contrast, Western countries emphasized lower-level education, and the number of universities in the entire country was not as many as in one corner of Shanghai. Therefore, education in those countries flourished, unlike China's unwieldy and chaotic situation. Furthermore, secondary education in China is becoming increasingly aristocratic and commercialized. Universities are established in large numbers, and secondary schools are like shops in a row. If you open one, I open one. Several can be found on one street. In general, those who run schools, in addition to cultivating personal influence, use this as a guise to profit from it. Tuition and other fees are extremely expensive. Since the goal is so base and vile, the content is naturally not worth mentioning. As long as you have money (袁頭，钞票也可), you can enter casually. Exams are a formality, and teachers are particularly flattering to students. Thinking about the label of "wild chicken schools," you can imagine that there are often dramas of randomly recruiting students. Under this kind of education system, if you are not a wealthy class with ample property, you cannot step into the gates of a secondary school, let alone dream of entering a university, because there are two invisible signs hanging there: "School area, the poor are not allowed to enter." In fact, your fate is determined in this way. The enjoyment of higher education and the exploration of profound theories are the exclusive rights of the wealthy class. The poor have no share and can only remain detached from learning like gazing at the ocean and sighing. Therefore, I want to find a way to remedy this, namely, to establish public libraries, so that the poor who are eager to learn but have no money to go to school can also have some opportunities to study on their own under the pressure of life.

People say that West Lake is most beautiful in spring, but I love suburban outings in the cool autumn. The jade plate (moon) has not yet fallen, and I still doubt it is summer. The golden millet is just beginning to contain (seeds), and I am beginning to feel autumn. Snowy lotus roots and green water chestnuts are good for side dishes. Cloud pines and purple chestnuts each form a ball. At this time, I alone embrace the moon over the calm lake, and the rushing tide flows against the current.

Science

Methods for Making Ink and Ink Remover 115

— Shi Dong

Ink existed in our country about three thousand years ago. In the West, Egypt also had ink made from coal and oil very early. In the eleventh century, someone made ink using a compound of tannic acid and iron. However, its quality was not as good as today's ink. As for the ink we use now, it is the result of long-term research by many scholars, and it was improved about seventy-three years ago by a person named Lienhard.

Ink Making Method: The most important chemicals are tannic acid and ferrous sulfate. Originally, ink could be made with just these two chemicals, but to prevent precipitation and mold, some other chemicals must be added. Moreover, there is a certain amount and many methods. Now the chemicals and amounts are written below:

Tannic acid 23.4 grams, gallic acid 7.7 grams, ferrous sulfate 30.0 grams, hydrochloric acid 2.5 grams, gum arabic 10.0 grams, carbolic acid 1.0 gram, water 1000.0 grams

What is mixed like this is colorless ink, that is, it must wait until after writing to turn black. Therefore, a few grams of aniline must be added, then blue-black ink can be made.

Method for Making Red Ink

The method for making red ink is extremely simple. The chemicals are as follows:

Red dye EOSIN 20 grams, gum arabic 20 grams, alcohol 50 grams, a small amount of carbolic acid, water 1000 grams

Method for Making Purple Ink

Methyl 10 grams, sugar 10 grams, oxalic acid 2 grams, water 1000 grams

Method for Making Ink Remover

Mixing citric acid, tartaric acid, and oxalic acid in equal parts can make ink remover.

Method for Making Ink Remover Powder

If the ink has not dried and you want to remove the words on the paper, the ink remover will lose its function. Therefore, alum, amber, and sulfur must be mixed in equal parts, and then wiped on the paper with silk or cotton to remove the words on the paper.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Suggestions for Improving Women's Clothing 116

— Jing Yu

Men's clothing has already been suggested for improvement by Mr. Zhang Cangsu, but women's clothing, although Mr. Huai Jingcheng has suggested improvements, only improved a portion of the shorts, which is not a thorough solution. Because women's clothing fundamentally needs improvement, and cannot be ignored, therefore, I will list my humble opinions as follows:

Women's clothing in our country today can be described as the ultimate spectacle of splendor and strangeness. As for non-Chinese and non-Western, also Chinese and also Western, they mostly bring forth the new from the old, and boast of novelty and strangeness. There are also so-called new clothing companies that fuel the trend and actively promote it. The materials must be imported, and the manufacturing method must admire Europeanization, turning our country's inherent silk fabrics into high shelves, resulting in panic of overproduction. On the one hand, it fosters women's extravagant psychology and bad habits, leading to various malpractices such as economic oppression, moral degradation, and family changes.

Taking the clothing materials for summer now as an example, most fashionable women use a kind of gauze silk as thin as cicada wings. This kind of gauze silk comes from Europe and America, and its value is extremely high. Clothes made from it are indeed as light as mist and exceptionally cool,

, but the muscles are exposed, and young people are tempted by them, and thus stray into the wrong path. There are many such people, and nothing is more destructive to morality than this!

Even the commonly worn cheongsam is nothing but a continuation of the old customs of the Manchu Qing Dynasty (because it is the clothing of the banner people, so it is called cheongsam). Under this revolutionary trend, there is no room for it to exist. Moreover, the real cheongsam is still broad and suitable for the body, but the currently popular cheongsam has long been changed to have a slender waist and narrow sleeves, looking unlike anything. How can it be comfortable to wear on the body? In addition, most of its hemlines have no slits, or if they do, they are only two or three inches high, which is equivalent to not having any. Therefore, movement is not convenient, and it is especially difficult to get on and off boats and cars. I remember a woman who was catching a boat in the Huangpu River the year before last. Just as she was about to board the boat, she fell into the river because she was wrapped in the hem of her cheongsam and could not take a big step, and she died instantly. From this point of view, this kind of clothing is more harmful than beneficial! In ancient times, strange clothing was punishable. The clothing worn by women today is considered strange clothing! It can be said to be on the list of punishable items!

Based on the above reasons, women's clothing should be improved. As for the degree of improvement, in my opinion, it may be based on the old-fashioned dress as a standard, and with careful consideration of the advantages and disadvantages, so that the women of the whole country, with their tops and skirts, tend to be consistent. Wearing them will not feel inconvenient, and there will be no danger of falling. In terms of appearance, it is also quite dignified and generous, without being inelegant at all. In terms of material selection, the government should issue a clear order to promote and limit the use of domestic silk fabrics, and absolutely prohibit the use of foreign goods, so that domestic goods can be sold well and the leakage can be stopped. Whether it is appropriate or not, please submit it to all members for common discussion, and I hope for it very much.

A Tragic Scene

Aunt 117

— Ling

When I heard that my aunt had passed away from this world, I was in a daze of sorrow for several days!

I thought of her gray hair, her pale face, her soft palms, her simple and clean house and bedroom. Everything that my mind could remember, everything about my aunt, I thought of it all! When I thought of all these things, it was as if I had lost something in my soul, and it was extraordinarily uncomfortable and empty!

Having lost my mother before I was four years old was truly very pitiful and pitiable! I think, if there had not been someone like my aunt to raise me at that time, I really don't know what kind of person I would have become! I think, if I can still say that I have a little intelligence now, then it is clearly given to me by my dear aunt. At the same time, I believe that if I have a recognition of "love," then it was also only given to me by my aunt. Besides my approachable aunt, who else has ever given me a kind look!

What contrasts very well with this is my uncle's violence! Although he died the second year after I came to his house, the scenes of him often, after drinking alcohol, venting his anger on me as a vent, will forever, like a poisonous snake, bite into my heart, and I will never forget them no matter what!

"You jinx, who wants you to come to my house? Your mother has already been killed by you (I heard that my horoscope is very strong, and my mother was killed by my strong destiny), your family has already been broken up by you, and now you want to break up our family too? You jinx! ... Jinx! ..."

Such venomous and fierce curses often made me cry and cry; although my aunt gently pulled me to her side or to the kitchen, using gentle words to comfort me, my uncle's curses would still continue. Sometimes he would use a threatening tone, saying, "If you cry again! ... If you don't stop crying! ... You crying jinx! ... I really have to beat you to death! ,

...", often scaring me so much that I dared not cry out but coughed uncontrollably!

Really, in those days when I had lost my own mother, and my father had no choice but to work as a hired worker for his own livelihood and was unable to raise me, my aunt was able to raise me regardless of my uncle's complaints. This truly makes me yearn for her more and more!

I think my aunt loved me so much perhaps because she had no children of her own! When I was studying in elementary school, she always encouraged me: "A Ling, you must study hard! For your poor father, for your broken family, for your future career!" At that time, I was petted like a docile lamb, and I went to school to study every day without stopping! Although my body is very weak now, I don't dare to complain about her teaching me to be so docile. Especially when the semester exams were over and I returned home with the prizes I had won, my aunt would always hold me tightly, desperately caressing my face! Her happy smile contained clear and bitter tears! Sometimes she would suddenly ask me:

"A Ling, when you grow up and become successful, will you still remember your aunt?" When I replied loudly and playfully, "I will," she would laugh heartily.

"You must remember, A Ling."

Sometimes she would be so happy that she would be in a daze, holding my hands tightly, her eyes looking up at the sky, as if that distant future would definitely have a beautiful and happy situation! After she came out of her daze, she would passionately hug me, kiss me, and caress me!

But now? She was squeezed to death by a life of poverty. All the hopes and desires she had yearned for in her life were ultimately destroyed under the iron heel of reality! Therefore, when she took her last breath, she was also full of tears. Alas! How cruel and tragic this is!
