Public Notice of Service ▲ Regarding the case of public notice of service, Changyi Firm and Hong Yousheng, due to the debt case, the original copy of the judgment could not be served because the defendant Hong Yousheng was missing. Later, according to the plaintiff Changyi Firm's request for public notice of service, it has been ruled to be approved. Now, the original copy of the judgment to be received by the defendant is specially given public notice of service in accordance with Article 152 of the Civil Procedure Regulations. One original copy of the judgment is issued. Right, the defendant Hong Yousheng is notified ▲ Regarding the case of public notice of service, China Business Company and Ruiji Store owner Cai Ruiming et al., due to the rent arrears case, the original copy of the judgment could not be served because the defendant Ruiji Store owner Cai Ruiming et al. was missing. Later, according to the plaintiff's request for public notice of service, it has been ruled to be approved. Now, the original copy of the judgment to be received by the defendant is specially given public notice of service in accordance with Article 153 of the Civil Procedure Regulations. One original copy of the judgment is issued. Right, the defendants Ruiji Store owner Cai Ruiming, Pingji Store owner Qu Kunfan, and Yutai Store owner Qu Dongyu are notified ▲ Regarding the case of public notice of service, Gu Zhu Shi v. Yang Gengxi et al. for assault, the original copy of the judgment could not be served because the addresses of the plaintiff and the defendants were unknown. Now, in accordance with Article 199, Paragraph 1, and Article 200, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, public notice of service is specially given. You are hereby notified. Two summons are issued. Right, the plaintiff and defendants Gu Zhu Shi, Yang Gengxi, and Zhu Sanxiao are notified

Shanghai Local Court 119

Criminal Judgments ▲ Judgment on the case of Dai San et al. for theft (Main Text) Dai San, Li Xiaoliuzi, Zhao Xiaorenzi, Li Xiaoerzi, and the other four persons are sentenced to six months of imprisonment each for colluding to commit theft, with a three-year probation period for each. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days ▲ Judgment on the case of Zhang Fusheng et al. for theft (Main Text) Zhang Fusheng and Yu Ruimei are sentenced to six months of imprisonment each for jointly breaking and entering theft. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days ▲ Judgment on the case of Chen Qigao for opium (Main Text) Chen Qigao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan for providing a house for others to smoke opium, and sentenced to three months of imprisonment for smoking opium. The combined sentence is seven months of imprisonment and a fine. If the fine is paid through compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment can be converted for one yuan. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days ▲ One opium lamp, one opium pipe, and one opium probe/cigarette holder, six pieces in total, and opium ash are confiscated and burned together ▲ Judgment on the case of Yuan Fuda for opium (Main Text) Yuan Fuda is fined forty yuan for possessing opium with the intent to commit a crime. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment can be converted for one yuan. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one yuan of fine for one day. One small box of opium paste, one small pack of opium ash, and one small piece of opium confiscated ▲ Judgment on the case of Lu Wenming et al. for opium (Main Text) Lu Wenming and Peng Yuangen are sentenced to one month of imprisonment each for smoking opium and fined thirty yuan. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment can be converted for one yuan. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days or one yuan of fine for one day. Chuande Wu is acquitted. Two opium pipes, one opium lamp dish, one opium probe/cigarette holder, one opium brush, one opium pot, and one opium box with a little ash inside are confiscated ▲ Judgment on the case of Chen Qichang et al. for opium (Main Text) Chen Qichang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing a house for others to smoke opium with intent to profit, and sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for smoking opium. The combined sentence is seven months of imprisonment and a fine of thirty yuan. Ge Sanbao is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for smoking opium. If the fine is not paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment can be converted for one yuan. The number of days of detention before the final judgment is used to offset one day of imprisonment for two days or one yuan of fine for one day. Opium paraphernalia confiscated as per the list
